Muslims Commemorate Martyrs of Yuguan This Morning 104

The hall is located in the Qinglian Street Mosque. The Central Government sent Wu Tiecheng to offer sacrifices.

The Shanghai Muslims' memorial service for Battalion Commander An Dexin, who died in Yuguan, and the soldiers who died in battle, is scheduled to be held at 9:00 AM this morning at the Qinglian Street Mosque in Fangbang Bridge. The Central Executive Committee and Chairman Lin of the National Government specially sent Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city as a representative to offer sacrifices. Representatives from Muslim communities from all over the country also arrived and reported to the meeting before 8:00 PM yesterday. Details are as follows:

Venue Arrangement 105

The entrance of the Qinglian Street Mosque was decorated with plain colors yesterday afternoon. The hall was set up in the playground, with a mat shed on top and a platform in the middle. Plain banners and elegiac couplets were hung all around. The hall is quite large and can accommodate more than 1,000 people.

Meeting Staff 106

The meeting staff was elected yesterday, including the presidium members Ma Liang, Ha Shaofu, Huang Zhenpan, the general secretary Ma Tianying, the master of ceremonies Wang Hongjun, the chief receptionists Wu Yongxia, Lu Zhongxiang, Xu Shaoxian, and more than a dozen receptionists.

Meeting Agenda 107

1. Ring the bell to start the meeting; 2. All stand at attention; 3. Pay the highest respects to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier; 4. Read the Premier's will respectfully; 5. Silence; 6. Report the purpose of the meeting; 7. All stand up; 8. Recite the Quran; 9. Lamentation; 10. Report the deeds of the martyred soldiers; 11. Guest speeches; 12. Photography; 13. Adjournment.

Meeting Elegy 108

Alas, foreign enemies are encroaching, and the national situation is becoming increasingly critical. Ever since September 18th, the powerful invaders have been rampaging, constantly expanding their continental policy, hoping to destroy our country's ambitions. This time, when they invaded Yuguan, our An Dexin unit, guarding the territory, resolutely led their entire battalion of brave soldiers and swore to fight to the death, ultimately leading to the defeat of the many by the few, perishing with the city. Alas, the great righteousness is awe-inspiring and shines like the sun and moon. The heroic deeds are a lesson for future generations. Everyone must die, but there are deaths heavier than Mount Tai or lighter than a feather. Things do not necessarily involve calculating gains and losses, and success or failure should not be discussed in terms of heroes. The martyr An did not act carelessly when facing the crisis, shedding his blood on the majestic pass, achieving benevolence and taking righteousness, and being loyal to the Party and the country. His name will be remembered forever. Although defeated, he is still glorious, enough to influence future generations. This is how we know that the spirit of the martyr An and all the patriotic brave soldiers is immortal. However, the reason why we deeply mourn the martyr An is not only because of his death for justice, but only Yuguan has not yet been restored, leaving the martyr An with empty regrets. Therefore, we offer this elegy, saying: Alas, General, a man of great hope for saving the times, sitting and guarding the border, the chickens and dogs are silent. You uniquely exercised your authority, and the barbarians were conquered, and the court and the countryside admired you together. Alas, the Japanese bandits invaded our Yuguan, and with a cry, the three armies were ordered to fight. We were hoping that the invaders would be taught a lesson, but unexpectedly, the red-hot heart was suddenly shot through. Three thousand sons and brothers died with you. Such magnificence and grandeur are unmatched in ancient times. It is recorded in history books that even though the person is dead, the name remains. The spirit is immortal, shining with the sun and the moon. But the star of the general has suddenly fallen, who will fight for the nation and bring glory? The national crisis is severe, who will resist for China? With tears, we present this elegy, hoping that you will not abandon it and come and enjoy it.

Meeting Declaration 109

Alas, the Northeast has been lost and has not yet been recovered. The hated Ezo barbarians have insatiable greed, constantly encroaching and oppressing us. After occupying our Liaodong, they invaded Rehe. After our righteous army did their best to resist, they could not develop and changed their strategy to attack our Yuguan. Yuguan is a natural barrier, the throat of Pingjin. If Yuguan is lost, Rehe and Mongolia will be in danger. Fortunately, our Lord An Dexin led 500 brave soldiers to resist them outside the national gate, slightly blunting the enemy's edge. Ultimately, due to weak troops and limited strength, the ammunition was exhausted and aid was cut off, and he died in battle on the battlefield. His loyal and courageous spirit fills the universe and is enough to shame those who possess heavy troops and treat their territory like worn-out shoes. When Lord An waved his spear to resist the enemy, he forgot himself for loyalty and forgot his family for the country, using his horse armor to wrap his body and taking the battlefield as his pleasure. Such loyal and righteous people are rare throughout history. In the distant past, he can be compared with Yan Pingyuan, Changshan, and Qi Jiguang, and in recent times, he can be mentioned in the same breath as Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai. Lord An was a believer in the pure religion of Islam, with extraordinary ambitions and the ability to build a bright and upright career, enjoying the great name of loyalty and martyrdom for thousands of years. Although Yuguan has fallen, the merits and achievements of Lord An shine in the annals of history. This is why we mourn Lord An and commemorate Lord An today.

Biography of Martyr An 110

The martyr's family belonged to Baoding, Hebei, and was a follower of the Islamic religion. He had an 80-year-old mother, a brother, a wife, two daughters, and a son. His family worked as farmers. The martyr had great ambitions since childhood, saddened by the decline of China, the rapid encroachment of enemies, and the deep disaster. Therefore, he engaged in military service, vowing to repay the country with iron and blood. He entered the Northeast Jiangwu Hall Infantry Department and graduated in the summer of the 16th year of the Republic. He served as a major battalion commander of the 23rd Division of the 29th Army and the adjutant of this division. In the 18th year of the Republic, it was reorganized into the 9th Independent Brigade of Infantry. The martyr served as the lieutenant colonel battalion commander of the 1st Battalion of the 626th Regiment of the brigade. During the September 18th and January 28th incidents, the martyr witnessed the rampant behavior of the eastern neighbor and the fragmentation of the mountains and rivers. He ground his teeth and trained his subordinates, brave soldiers, vowing to avenge this hatred. When the Yuguan war broke out, the martyr was secretly pleased and said to his soldiers, "It is time for us to repay the country!" He led 500 brave soldiers to guard the South City Gate, and there was a heroic saying: "If you want to break Yuguan, you must pass through the corpse of Dexin!" His tone was generous and passionate, and those who heard it were indignant. On January 1st, the Japanese army used its giant cannons and the cover of tanks to attack fiercely. Martyr An fought against a force of 2,000 with 500 soldiers, using rifles and machine guns against their giant cannons and powerful weapons, disregarding his own life. The sharpness of the weapons was not comparable, and the number of soldiers was vastly different. When reinforcements did not arrive and the ammunition was exhausted, he still shouted with his bare hands and fought the enemy in close combat, causing 500 brave soldiers to regard death as home. In the end, he died in battle in the wilderness of the north. Alas, the death of the martyr is not only the glory of the country but also the glory of the world's Muslims.

Brief History of Martyrdom 111

After the Japanese army threw grenades and bombed the temporary residence of the Japanese military police team at the Yuguan Railway Station on the night of January 1, they sent troops to harass and shell. Therefore, our army not only sent people to negotiate with the Japanese side but also stepped up vigilance. The next day (January 2), as soon as it dawned, more than 200 armed Japanese soldiers gathered under the South City Gate and climbed the city with ladders. The first battalion of An Dexin guarded the South Gate. The Japanese army climbed the city and fired guns and cannons at the city. The troops stationed in our city did not receive orders at the time, so they were not able to return fire and could only throw bricks and tiles. Later, because the Japanese army's artillery fire became more intense, our defending soldiers could no longer bear it and began to fire machine guns, sweeping down the city. For a time, the Japanese army suffered heavy casualties and began to retreat. Subsequently, the Japanese army repeatedly attacked the city several times and were repelled. On the morning of the 3rd, after the Japanese army bombed the South Gate with heavy artillery, our first battalion piled up sacks at the damaged area to provide cover and continued to resist calmly. After a while, the Japanese army sent a tank leading more than 300 infantrymen to attack the city. After the enemy's tanks crashed through our army's sack cover, they attacked into the city. Our soldiers dodged the tanks and desperately charged at their infantry. At this time, although the Japanese soldiers were once again charged out of the city by our first battalion, the strength of our South Gate was mostly killed or injured. Battalion Commander An Dexin then requested that the third battalion, which was guarding the East Gate, dispatch a part of its troops to arrive at the South Gate for assistance. Before the reinforcements arrived, the Japanese army advanced on a large scale. At that time, because the Japanese army's artillery fire was exceptionally fierce, our soldiers suffered too many casualties, and Battalion Commander An was also seriously injured. He retreated from the West Water Gate to outside the city and died for his country. Alas, the loyal and courageous martyr An and all the officers and soldiers of the entire battalion ultimately shed their last drop of blood at the West Gate.

Wu Tiecheng's elegiac couplet says, "A small force defends the border, and when the enemy comes, they kill them, vowing to fight to the end, and their blood stains the dust. In the face of adversity, their loneliness and loyalty are to be admired, but public justice and the League of Nations are looked upon in vain. Their strength is not enough, but their righteousness is unwavering. The land is full of heroes, and their heroic spirit will inspire Yuguan for thousands of years." The Liaohai mountains are covered with clouds, and hearing the wind, they will raise their arms and sing sadly." Talks about moving the artifacts of the Forbidden City to Kaifeng and Luoyang. The plan for organizing Sichuan's government has been drafted. Artifacts Decided to Move to Kaifeng and Luoyang According to Chu, the central government has decided to move the artifacts of the Forbidden City to Kaifeng and Luoyang. The Executive Yuan, following the central government's order, has telegraphed the Kaifeng authorities to select an appropriate location for the artifacts to be transported to Kaifeng for safekeeping. The 2,118 boxes of artifacts that have arrived in Pukou will be temporarily stopped at Pukou Station. Once the location for safekeeping has been selected, they will be moved for preservation.

Plan for Organizing Sichuan's Government Regarding the recent disputes in Sichuan Province, the 330th meeting of the Central Political Conference decided to entrust the Executive Yuan with the task of detailing the implementation measures based on the National Government's order of the 17th year of the Republic and drafting a plan. The Executive Yuan, based on this resolution of the Central Political Conference, has begun to draft the plan for organizing Sichuan's government. Once it is completed, it will be submitted to the Central Political Conference for approval and then handed over to Zhang Yuejun to take to Sichuan to implement in conjunction with the Sichuan authorities. As for the establishment of Xikang Province, a decision will be made after Zhang Yuejun inspects Sichuan. The Liu Case Was Handed Over to the Disciplinary Committee The National Government has handed over the case of the Jiangsu Provincial Government shooting Liu Yusheng to the National Government's Political Official Disciplinary Committee for review. In addition to forwarding the Jiangsu Provincial Government's reply to the Supervisory Yuan, the Executive Yuan has no opinion on this case. The Jiangsu Provincial Government's reply stated that Liu Yusheng was a communist and that there was a record of his case in the 16th year of the Republic. This time, the execution was approved by the Martial Law Headquarters and the Military Commission and was unrelated to the Jiangsu Provincial Government. It is heard that the Jiangsu Provincial Government will submit a second reply to defend itself. As for whether political prisoners from the 16th year of the Republic are excluded from the amnesty, I have not checked the amnesty provisions in detail and cannot answer.

The Taxpayers' Association Sends a Letter to the Public Works Bureau to Pay Attention

From 2 yuan to more than 20 yuan. According to the monthly rent received, a total of 49 yuan, the water bill paid, from the time of renting until October last year, was at least 2 yuan or more per month, and at most 3 yuan and 40 cents. The bill in December was even more drastic, reaching more than 20 yuan. The National Coal Relief Association Discusses in Detail. As for the measures to reorganize and reduce costs, the association proposed a detailed discussion when it convened the National Coal Relief Conference in October last year, and it is in the process of planning.

New Methods for Sugar and Northern Goods. The new methods formulated by the Northern Goods Industry Association are as follows: Scale Discount 1. 88% discount for selling Southern standards; 2. 85% discount for selling Northern standards; 3. Other items such as red and black [items] that are usually weighed [amount] will continue to be calculated at 98% discount; 4. All current 98% discounts for Southern standards will be cancelled; 5. All items such as [items] sold using Southern standards will be discounted 88% including the skin. Payment Terms: (A) The following terms are set for sales to various domestic customer groups: 1. For Southern standards, payment is due one month from the date of shipment, with payment due every ten days at the end of the month, using ten-day drafts; 2. For Northern standards, payment is due on the 20th of the month for goods shipped from the 1st to the 10th, and payment is due at the end of the month for goods shipped from the 11th to the 20th, all using ten-day drafts; the rest can be deduced by analogy. (B) The following terms are set for sales to export groups: 1. Payment for the Guangzhou, Shantou, and Xiamen groups is due seven days from the date of shipment, using ten-day drafts; 2. For the Fuzhou, Xinghua, Quanzhou, Wenzhou, Ningbo, and Yangtze groups, payment is due on the 20th of the month for goods shipped from the 1st to the 10th, and payment is due at the end of the month for goods shipped from the 11th to the 20th, all using ten-day drafts; the rest can be deduced by analogy. The above regulations are scheduled to be implemented from January 26, 1933. As for the [industry] Association, the methods are roughly the same as those of the Northern Goods Association, so they are omitted.

Southern Goods Insist on Opposition. The Southern Goods Industry Association believes that the [industry] and the Northern Goods Industry have taken advantage of the implementation of the city weighing to formulate new methods, shorten the payment period, and require that all payments that previously used checks must be changed to drafts. They have also formulated other discounts. Compared with the old system, it is calculated that each load will be short by one and a half catties. They believe that this is very unfair. Therefore, the Southern Goods Industry Association and the customer groups have jointly opposed it, demanding fair transactions. They should obey the use of city weighing, but the discounts should be based on the original standards. The Northern Goods Industry refused to withdraw the new methods, resulting in a major dispute.

Meeting Resolves Important Matters. After the Southern Goods Industry Association held a meeting and made a decision, it immediately issued an emergency notice to its members, which read: "Notice: The sugar industry and the northern goods industry have formulated new discounts and changed to drafts for the trial use of city weighing. This association has repeatedly convened emergency meetings and resolved that the city weighing should be based on 96% of the original standard, and all other [methods] should be denied. Now, in order to actively implement the methods, a general meeting of members was convened yesterday and resolved: 1. Before this association and the other party have resolved the matter, it is forbidden to enter the market or privately buy goods from the upper companies. Anyone who violates the resolution will have their deposit confiscated in full and their membership revoked. 2. In order to prepare for the aftermath, each member is allowed to pay a deposit of 100 yuan, which will be kept by the custodial committee and returned in full afterwards. The custodial committee will be [names] of the American Concession, the British Concession, and [names] of the French Concession, and [names] of Zhabei. Members are requested to pay the custodial committee near them within two days. The office of this association is temporarily located in the New Music Men's Business Association on Nanyang Bridge, French Concession. If you have any business, please go there. This is a record and announcement, and it is hoped that you will follow it. This matter concerns the fundamental interests of this industry. It is hoped that members will resolutely stand to the end and not act against it. This is most important. This notice is hereby issued."

Yesterday's Market Situation. Since the Southern Goods Industry resolved to strike, the marine products, sugar, and northern goods industries in the United Market on Xiaodongmen Zhonghua Road operated as usual yesterday, but there were no transactions. The Southern Goods Industry Association specially appointed [list of names] to be responsible for handling this matter and set up an office on Nanyang Bridge.

Sending Personnel to Investigate the Truth. After receiving the report, the City Chamber of Commerce immediately sent staff member Yuan Hongjun to the relevant industry associations at 10:00 a.m. yesterday to investigate the reasons for the strike of the Southern Goods Industry. After receiving the report, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs also sent staff members to thoroughly investigate the matter in order to find a way to mediate and avoid expanding the dispute.

Puyi Real Estate Company Shareholder Meeting 130

Puyi Real Estate Company, located at 50 Nanjing Road in this city, convened its annual shareholder meeting yesterday on the third floor of the company. Chairman Dong [blank] Wen [blank] read the business report for the 21st year, which stated briefly: This year's business was very quiet due to the impact of the September 18th Incident last year. Although there is a lot of silver stored in Shanghai, capitalists are wary of investing in businesses due to the current situation. As a result, the construction industry has not made much progress, and real estate transactions, from an investment perspective, are almost at a standstill. However, there have been quite a few transactions of commercial and residential properties, with a total value of approximately [blank] 18 million taels.

Business Situation: This year, two new properties were purchased, both for expanding existing bases, requiring 39,000 taels of silver. Furthermore, 15 properties were sold, totaling 275,696.74 taels of silver. The construction department handled a total of 38 projects, of which 16 were built by the company itself, and the rest were built on behalf of other parties, valued at [blank] 577,000 taels. The company's construction value also reached 545,000 [blank] taels. The two items totaled 1,122,000 [blank] taels. The entire design, sampling, and supervision of these projects were undertaken by the company's construction department. The largest project this year was the Dahua Apartment located on Jing'an Temple Road, which was completed in early September. By the end of the year, 80-90% of it was rented out. The company's property acquisition has always been based on the standard of good location and rising land prices, and the acquired properties are developed as much as possible to increase income. As of the end of the year, the total value of these real estate properties was 16,123,472.25 taels, of which housing properties accounted for 12,566,029.48 taels, accounting for 77.94%, and land properties accounted for 3,530,902 taels, accounting for approximately 21.90%. Properties under construction accounted for 26,540.77 taels, accounting for approximately 0.16%. The total value of the above-mentioned real estate has been depreciated, calculated at the usual 4%, totaling 166,648.96 taels. Most of the company's properties are located in the Puyi Model Village and the bustling areas within the two concessions. As for the locations of all properties, the details are as follows in percentage: Public Concession 55.40%, French Concession 29.68%, Puyi Model Village 8.88%, Other Locations 6.04%. There are three properties in other locations, one on French Central Street in Tianjin, and the other two in the Special Second District of Hankou.

Comparison of Development: Since 1919, the company's growth has been even more [blank] progressive. According to the financial statements of the most recent three years, the value of its real estate and the annual rent collection are compared and listed as follows: At the end of 1919, 9,713,974.07 taels, at the end of 1920, 14,882,861.22 taels, and at the end of 1921, 16,123,472.25 taels. The comparison of rental income is as follows: 230,690.59 taels in 1919, 631,153.82 taels in 1920, and 708,943.80 taels in 1921.

Reserve Amount: The company's reserve fund totaled 1,033,763.19 taels by the end of the year. All depreciation on housing properties of 166,648.96 taels and depreciation on income-generating assets of 65,000.00 taels have been deducted from the asset accounts. In addition to the above-mentioned reserve fund, there is also an intangible reserve fund, which is the difference between the book value of the company's real estate and the market value estimated in May 1921. At that time, the book value, excluding depreciation, was 15,494,167.10 taels, while the price estimated based on market value was 19,164,228.00 taels. The difference between the two is 3,670,060.90 taels, accounting for about 23.68% of the total assets.

Last Year's Account Summary: This year, the company's net profit was 170,402.95 taels, plus 660,176.31 taels carried over from last year's profit and loss account, totaling 830,579.26 taels. The board of directors has allocated and paid the following: 191,996.64 taels for year-end dividends and cash bonuses paid on February 5, 1921; 60,174.93 taels transferred to the reserve fund account on April 13, 1921; 35,860.32 taels paid on June 30 for the semi-annual dividend of 6% on Class B preferred shares; 35,959.68 taels paid on December 31 for the semi-annual dividend of 6% on Class B preferred shares; 57,600.00 taels paid on December 31 for the annual dividend of 8% on Class A preferred shares. The remaining balance is 448,987.69 taels. On January 11 this year, the board of directors approved the distribution of a dividend of 7% to ordinary shareholders, which will cost 134,398.65 taels.

After Mr. Lei finished his report, all the accounts were approved by the entire body. The board of directors then thanked the shareholders for their enthusiastic support and all the staff for their loyal service. Finally, they rigorously recommended the company's staff and accountants before adjourning.

Yan E's "Shanghai Commercial Practices" Published 131

Divided into Twenty-Two Categories, with Forty-Two Types of Industry Regulations.

Yan E, secretary of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and director of the Commercial Monthly Magazine, was formerly a professor at the National Shanghai College of Commerce. He has served commercial organizations in this city for over ten years. Recently, due to frequent requests from courts, lawyers, and commercial organizations in various provinces and cities to investigate various commercial customs in Shanghai as a basis for handling cases, he compiled a book titled "Shanghai Commercial Practices," based on the various inquiries answered or explained by the former Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai County Chamber of Commerce, Merchants Group Reorganization Committee, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Bankers' Association, Money Trade Association, and others. The book is published by the Publishing Department of the Xinsheng News Agency, located at 280 Wangping Street, Shanghai. The content is divided into twenty-two categories, including Ordering, Delivery, Returns, Documentary Bills, Mortgages, Commissions, Buying and Selling, Interest Rates, Negotiable Instruments, Contracts, Partnerships, Push Sales, Debts, Guarantees, Defaults, Partners, Transportation, Securities, Account Books, Leases, Business, and Industry Regulations. The Industry Regulations are all those approved and promulgated by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, totaling forty-two industries, including Banking, Money Trade, Silk [blank], Southern Goods, Timber, Coal, Tobacco Exchange, Miscellaneous [blank], [blank] Garden, Mercerized Cotton Weaving, etc. The entire book is over four hundred pages thick and includes a title inscription by Yu Qiaqing, a leader in the Shanghai business community, as well as prefaces by Wu Jingxiong, a member of the Legislative Yuan, Bei Kangsi, chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, Yan Yinwu, standing committee member of the National Lawyers Association, Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Xu Ji, standing committee member of the Bankers' Association, Qin Runqing, chairman of the Money Trade Association, lawyers Chen Rui, Li Zuyu, and accountants Xu Yongzuo, Pan Xulun, and Dai [blank], chief editor of the Banking Weekly. The book has now been published and sells for 1.50 yuan. The Xinsheng News Agency at 280 Wangping Street and the dispatch office of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce are all selling it.

Rich in Content, Price Remains the Same, Continuous Improvement, Unlimited Future

Da Wanbao is the most widely circulated and newest evening newspaper in this city. It was first published on this day last year (February 12, 1921). At that time, the Battle of Songhu was in full swing. The newspaper published a special issue for national [blank], assigning many war correspondents to enter and exit the front lines, probing for important news and publishing detailed daily reports, which were deeply welcomed by readers. Minutes of the Rice Milling Industry Association Meeting 133

The rice millers met the day before yesterday (the 10th), with Zhu Zixiang presiding. He reported on the matter of changing to new measuring instruments, which had been resolved and announced to the industry on January 31. However, the Bean and Rice Industry Association recently obtained approval to use a six-dou Shi Hu, which has been permitted by the Social Affairs Bureau. However, the national government has issued an order to unify the [blank] weights and measures system, which does not allow any [blank] deviation. He asked, "What will our industry do? Please discuss." It was resolved that since the Social Affairs Bureau has already approved it, the industry will also use the six-dou Shi Hu for sales in this area, and those selling bags will use 210 pounds as a standard, which is 1.2 Shi Hu. The market price will be calculated on a Shi Hu basis. It was also resolved to modify the machine labor regulations, stipulating that for bags shipped to Shanghai, unloading will start at 200 pounds, and machine labor will remain the same as before. For bulk shipments to Shanghai, unloading will be based on Shi Hu, and machine labor will be reduced by two cents. It was also resolved to calculate bran and broken rice based on the Shi Hu and market scale as usual.

Nail Manufacturers Discuss Joint Operations: China's machine-made round nails were first created by the Gongqin [blank] Factory in Yangshupu ten years ago. At that time, due to the raw materials for nail manufacturing being [blank] from abroad, the cost was too high, making it difficult to develop. Later, the factory repeatedly designed and presented proposals to the government to improve the tax system. In recent years, it has been able to compete with imported foreign nails in the market. However, newly established nail factories in this city have sprung up one after another. To date, there are more than ten factories, large and small. According to current statistics, production has suddenly become oversupplied. Therefore, there is some competition in business. Currently, the industry feels that the cost is high and the selling price is low, and that continuing in this way is not a good strategy. Therefore, members of the industry have convened a general meeting to negotiate a unified selling price and appoint representatives to contact foreign nail manufacturers to discuss cooperation methods. It is said that representatives of Chinese and foreign factories have met several times. The content and opinions of the organization have not yet been determined, but the Chinese factory side has reached a unanimous agreement on its aims.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks 138

Central Bank: 151st Inspection Report on Issuance Reserve. This association, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Law, is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the banknotes issued by this bank. The 151st inspection was conducted by Supervisor Wang Yihou at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on February 10, 1933. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of banknotes issued is 46,100,850 silver dollars, including 42,061,826 silver dollar notes and 4,046,224 subsidiary coin notes. The total amount of the banknote reserve is 46,100,850 silver dollars, including 37,959,050 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve is comprised of 33,986,140 silver dollars in the bank's issuance vault, 2,124,250 silver dollars in branches in various ports, and 1,848,660 silver dollars deposited with other banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 8,149,000 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold unit notes issued is 415,000. The total amount of the customs gold unit note reserve is 425,000, including US$170,000 deposited with other banks in this city, fixed at 40 customs gold units, totaling 425,000 customs gold units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guaranteed reserve 40%. The result of this inspection shows that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee does not reach 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is made on February 10, 1933, by the Central Bank Board of Supervisors.

China垦业 Bank: Inspection Report on Issuance Reserve. The issuance vault and business vault of China 垦业 Bank have always been completely separated. According to the bank's regulations, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guaranteed reserve below 30%. On the 11th of this month, Accountant Wang Zikang, together with Xu Ji, representative of the board of directors and supervisors, and Xu Busun, conducted an inspection. The results are as follows: the total amount of banknotes issued is 5,159,000 silver dollars. The total amount of banknote reserve is 5,159,000 silver dollars, including 4,130,388 silver dollars in cash reserve and 1,028,612 silver dollars in guaranteed reserve. The above two items show that the cash reserve accounts for slightly over 80% and the guaranteed reserve accounts for slightly less than 20%. This report is made accordingly.

Shipping Tycoon

Zheng Xitang Encounters Kidnappers for the Third Time, Shot in the Temple 140

Bodyguard, Russian Watchman, Saraeff Dies Defending Master, Two Police Officers Bravely Chase Kidnappers, Both Seriously Wounded, Zheng Xitang's Injuries are Very Severe, but Medical Treatment is Progressing Well.

Yesterday afternoon at around 2:00 PM, a shocking kidnapping case occurred near the Taikoo Wharf on the Bund in the Southern City (designated as Wharf No. 6 by the Public Works Department). The victim was Zheng Xitang, a well-known shipping tycoon from Ningbo who had twice escaped kidnapping attempts. This was, in fact, his third encounter. Although he was not taken by the bandits, Zheng was shot in the head and is in critical condition. His Russian bodyguard died on the spot after being shot in the temple. Two police officers from the First District General Office were seriously wounded while bravely pursuing the kidnappers. A stray bullet injured a worker. Three kidnappers were involved, all of whom escaped. The incident occurred in a densely populated area, yet the bandits dared to carry out a brazen kidnapping in broad daylight, shooting and injuring multiple people. This is unprecedented in the Southern City. The details are as follows:

Zheng Xitang's Business 141

Zheng Xitang, a renowned shipping magnate in Shanghai, is 41 years old and from Zhenhai, Zhejiang. He is the eldest of three siblings. His wife, Madam Li, passed away last year. They had four sons and two daughters. The eldest son and daughter are adults and married, while the rest are young. Zheng's shipping business in Shanghai can be considered groundbreaking. His most notable ventures include the Lao Gong Mao Steamboat Company in Dongjiadu, the Ping An Company at 214 Bund in the Southern City, the Tongyu Shipping Company at 170-178 Beijing Road in the Public Concession, and the large-scale shipyard in Bailianjing, Pudong, all of which were founded by Zheng himself. In addition, he has various other side businesses too numerous to mention.

Residing in Pudong to Avoid the Hustle and Bustle 142

Zheng is by nature thrifty, diligent, and self-disciplined, with a strong sense of responsibility. He personally manages all his businesses and spares no effort. Seeing that Shanghai's west side was too bustling, he moved to Bailianjing in Pudong to avoid the noise. However, he personally goes to the Shanghai Awakening Steamboat Company every day to work, without fail, even in heavy wind and rain. Zheng rises at dawn every day, eats a quick meal, and comes to Puxi. He first goes to his office on Beijing Road, and after lunch, he goes to the Ping An Company in the Southern City. After finishing his work, he still needs to go to various places to handle trivial matters, returning home late at night. He is so diligent. Due to his busy work schedule, he only owns a small Austin car for transportation, license number 7021 in the concession (city number 5370).

One Aborted Kidnapping 143

Zheng's reputation has been increasing daily, but it has attracted the attention of bandits. It is recalled that in October 1930, Zheng encountered kidnappers near the Dada Wharf in the Southern City. At the time, the bandits were trying to force Zheng into a car parked nearby, but Zheng struggled with all his might. One bandit fired a shot at Zheng, and the bullet pierced Zheng's fur coat, luckily hitting a diary in his pocket, preventing him from being injured. Zheng then suddenly bit the wrist of the bandit holding the gun, causing the bandit to drop the gun out of pain. Zheng picked it up and threw it into the Huangpu River. At the same time, detectives arrived after hearing the news and arrested one bandit on the spot. The bandit was later executed.

Daughter Kidnapped Twice 144

After that, Zheng received letters from the bandits with various threats, but he ignored them. He then encountered danger in the concession once, but escaped unharmed. Not long after, one of Zheng's sons and daughters were approached by kidnappers at the school gate. The son escaped, but the daughter was abducted, though she was released within ten days. Since then, Zheng hired a Russian watchman, Saraeff, as a bodyguard and obtained a self-defense pistol (gun serial number 443803) to protect him at all times. Therefore, although the bandits had designed many times, they were never successful.

Loyal and Brave Russian Watchman Saraeff

Kidnapping Attempt Yesterday 145

Yesterday afternoon, at around 1:00 PM, Zheng went to the Ping An Company in the Southern City as usual. After finishing his work at 2:50 PM, Zheng arranged to go elsewhere with the deputy manager, Chen Yisheng. Just as Zheng and Chen were about to get into the car, and the bodyguard Saraeff was closing the car door, three kidnappers suddenly jumped out from the side of the road. One was burly and wore a gray cloth robe, one wore a dark blue cotton robe, and one wore a cloth robe with a plain-colored vest and a velvet hat. One bandit rushed to Saraeff, threatening him with a gun. Another bandit forced Deputy Manager Chen Yisheng out of the car and ordered him to go upstairs immediately.

Bodyguard Dies 146

Seeing that they had encountered bandits, Chen had no choice but to get out of the car and quickly go upstairs. He blew his police whistle wildly, but just as the whistle sounded, gunshots rang out downstairs. Three shots were heard, and Zheng and Saraeff were lying in a pool of blood. When Chen went upstairs, the Russian Saraeff tried to draw his gun to resist, but one bandit struck first and shot Saraeff in the head. The bullet hit the right temple, and he fell to the ground instantly, with his brains splattered. He was sent to Tongren Hospital, but it was too late, and he died. Saraeff's self-defense pistol was taken by the bandits. At the same time, the third bandit dragged Zheng out of the car.

Victim Shot and Seriously Wounded 147

Because Zheng had encountered bandits several times before,

he had escaped because of resistance.

This time, he wanted to follow the previous example, hoping for a stroke of luck. Unexpectedly, he angered the bandit, who shot Zheng in the head. The bullet entered from the top of the head and did not penetrate. Zheng also fell into the blood. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, the bandits fled west along South Yangjiadu Street. At that time, Zhang Dianyong and Yang Zhanbiao, two patrol officers from the First District General Office, arrived after hearing the gunshots. The bandits turned north into Shi Xiang Gong Alley through Wai Ma Gua Street, then north to Lao Taiping Alley, and then to Dadongmen. At that time, there was a crowd of people watching a fight, and the bandits took the opportunity to mix into the crowd and escape without a trace.

Both Police Officers Shot 148

When the two police officers Zhang and Yang were chasing, the three bandits opened fire along the way. Officer Yang was shot in the left shoulder when he chased to Yangjiadu. Officer Zhang was also seriously injured in the right arm. However, the two police officers did not flinch and chased all the way to Dadongmen. After the bandits disappeared, they returned to the station to report. Both were sent to Shanghai Hospital. Officer Zhang's elbow was broken, and Officer Yang's injury was lighter. As for Zheng Xitang, he was taken to Shanghai Hospital by the car driver Zhang Arong after being injured. After the doctor examined him, he believed that his brain had been severely injured and his condition was critical.

Zheng Moans on the Sickbed 149

After Zheng arrived at the hospital, he lost consciousness due to excessive blood loss. He woke up a little while later. At that time, reporters had arrived after hearing the news. They saw Zheng wearing an old purple lambskin coat, white on top and black on the bottom, a flannel short shirt and woolen undershirt inside, black leather shoes, and a gray scarf. All of these were covered in blood. He was lying diagonally and moaning, constantly calling for a cotton quilt, as there was only a wooden board on the bed. Zheng's eyes were swollen, and blood was constantly flowing from the wound on the back of his head. At 3:20 PM, an ambulance from Tongren Hospital arrived, and the doctor also came.

Condition Progressing Well 150

After the doctor from Tongren Hospital arrived at Shanghai Hospital, he first checked his pulse and then opened his eyelids. He saw that his eyeballs were protruding outwards and said that he was afraid that there was no hope of survival. At the same time, Zheng's family and friends arrived one after another, earnestly requesting that he be rescued. The doctor said that the bullet must be removed as soon as possible by surgery to see how his condition changed before a solution can be found. After speaking, Zheng was carried into the ambulance on a stretcher and taken directly to Tongren Hospital. Last night, when reporters went to inquire, they were told that his condition was progressing well. Afterwards, it was found that when the bandits opened fire to resist arrest along the way, a passerby named Hu Desheng, 36 years old, from Yangzhou, who was a worker on the Haimen steamboat, was shot in the right arm and left leg by stray bullets and was also sent to Shanghai Hospital.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jianglun Transportation of Fish Changes Fee Dispute 151

Jiangsu and Jiangxin Detain More Than Two Hundred Buckets, Each Fish Store In Xiaodongmen Has Submitted An Negotiation. The Changjiang Steamship under China Merchants Steam Navigation Company transports fish from Hankou to Shanghai. The cost of each bucket is (dollars), the rest of the money is obtained by the crew and sailors. Now, the company is reorganizing the business and eliminating extra charges. From yesterday, staff members have been dispatched to detain the fish buckets transported on Jianglun, which has caused great disputes. The details are as follows:

Fish Transportation Fee: The fresh fish from Changjiang is transported to Shanghai. The fish store commissioned Changjiang boat to load the buckets and transport them there. The Changjiang boats under China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also transport this kind of goods. However, because they cannot be put in the cabin, they are mostly stacked on the deck and platform. Each fish store pays two dollars and two and a half dollars for each bucket. However, this is not counted into the company's freight, but is divided up among the sailors on the boat. When Li Weihou was the general manager last year, a transportation fee method was agreed upon with the boat owners and sailor captains of the Changjiang boat: half a dollar is paid for each bucket of fish to the captain, who then turns it over to the boat owner, and then to the company. This money is then used to prepare uniforms for the sailors. This has always been implemented accordingly.

Change the Method: Since Liu Hongsheng took over as general manager, he has been actively carrying out changes to the business of the Changjiang boats, prohibiting sailors from engaging in extra charges. The company believed that it was a big loss to have no freight income for the fresh fish transported to Shanghai. Therefore, it was decided that the transport of the fish buckets would be formally collected by the company. Therefore, each Jianglun boat was informed to obey it. However, the captains of each boat believed that since each fish bucket loaded on the boat had been paid five cents which was collected by the boat owner, how could the company not receive it? This transportation fee rate was agreed upon by the previous general manager and was not extra charges privately transported. Therefore, it will still be loaded as usual.

Detain the Fish and Goods: The company dispatched manager Li Rongsheng from the Southern Building yesterday to inspect the boat when the Changjiang boat arrived at port and detain each fish bucket. Manager Li then lead staff and workers to wait at Jinliyuan Pier. When Jiangjing boat arrived at the port, Li discovered sixty buckets of fresh fish, which he then detained, unloaded on land, and stored in the eighth cargo warehouse. At about 4 p.m., Jiangxin boat arrived at Shanghai, and Manager Li discovered a large batch of fresh fish, a total of one hundred and several ten buckets, which were also stored in Jinliyuan Pier.

Negotiations with Merchants: The fresh goods stores in Xiaodongmen followed customs and sent workers to the pier to pick up the goods in order to transport them to the store and put them up for sale. Because fresh goods must be picked up immediately and cannot be delayed for a moment, each merchant sent representatives to the South Warehouse to negotiate with Li to request the fish buckets. It was to no avail. Each merchant then negotiated with the company and believed that the transportation fee had already been paid. If the company believed that the procedure was not compliant, the boat owner was at fault, and the merchants' fish buckets should not be detained. When the reporter drafted this report, this matter had not yet been resolved.

Greyhound Association Discusses Reply to Tax Office's Question 152

The case is scheduled to continue tomorrow. The Greyhound Association is suing Martin, the current extra Chief Inspector of the Public Works Department, and McNaughton, the former General Director. The testimony of the plaintiff's witness, White Ash, mentioned stamp tax. The Director of the Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance, Xie Qi, stated that the Chinese government has never collected taxes on greyhounds and sent a letter to the association on the ninth, requesting that it make a statement based on the facts. After clarification, the association held a board meeting yesterday morning to discuss how to reply. A formal reply will be sent to the tax office within days. The situation discussed yesterday morning has not yet been released. It is said that the association may not be able to provide a detailed explanation before the end of the prosecution because it believed that since it had refused to explain at the time in court, if it were to publish it now, it would be suspected of contempt of court.

As for the trial, the defendant's lawyer, Hobru, continued to present his defense on the afternoon before yesterday until it was almost time to adjourn. The trial will continue on Monday, and the plaintiff's lawyer, Harshi, will respond.

The Shanghai Charity Organization Federation's temporary shelter in the Southern City of Shanghai has been established since last winter for over two months. A total of over 20,000 yuan has been spent on caring for the poor in the four shelters. Since spring has arrived and the weather has become warm, most of the poor have requested to leave the shelter and find their own way to make a living. However, there are still two thousand several hundred people remaining in the shelter. The shelter is short on funds and has difficulty providing supplies. Shih Hui-hsin Takes a Concubine; After a Month, the Concubine Returns to Ningbo and Insists on Leaving 156

Lived Together for Thirty-Nine Days, Then the Concubine Demanded to Leave

Shih, Unwilling in His Heart, Accused the Concubine of Colluding to "Release White Doves" [a euphemism for fraud]

The Concubine Said She Was Not Fully Developed and Could Not Bear the Pain

Shih Hui-hsin of Ningbo, currently 41 years old, resides at No. 30 in the Xinniu Company Lane in the French Concession. He is engaged in the copper and iron business and has accumulated some savings. He has a wife and a son. Because Shih needs to continue the line of his deceased father's side of the family, he considered taking a concubine. He revealed his intentions to others, asking them to find a suitable woman. In September of last year, Shih's friends Yuan Jinchun and Hua Juquan introduced a woman named Yao Caiyun (also known as Ruiyun), who was willing to become a concubine. Yao was only seventeen years old and had a beautiful appearance. After Shih examined her once, he found her satisfactory and paid a tea ceremony gift of 1,000 yuan. However, after she entered his household, they only lived together for thirty-nine days, when due to

sexual relations, she developed a strong aversion. Yao then returned to Ningbo. Shih hired lawyer Chen Wenxiang to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court, accusing Yao Ruiyun, Yao's parents Yao Bochun and Yao Lian, and the introducer Hua Juquan of colluding to defraud him of money. Attached was a civil lawsuit. The indictment stated: "Last September, Hua Juquan introduced Yao Bochun and his wife, fellow villagers, who intended to give their daughter Caiyun to be a concubine. The plaintiff, because he had to continue the line of Yao's father's side of the family, agreed to take her as a concubine. After several rounds of discussion, Caiyun agreed. On the 26th day of the tenth month of the same year, a voluntary agreement was written. The plaintiff paid

a tea ceremony gift of 1,000 yuan. Then, on the 31st day of the tenth month, he rented a house and lived with Caiyun. After she entered his household, he gave Caiyun an additional 400 yuan for savings. About 300 yuan was spent on clothing and miscellaneous items. On the 9th day of the twelfth month, Caiyun returned to her mother's house in Ningbo. Unexpectedly, he suddenly received a letter from lawyer Jiang Yiping, stating that he represented Yao Ruiyun and demanded to end the relationship. The plaintiff immediately checked his boxes and found that all 400 yuan in savings, as well as clothing, had been taken away. Thinking that Yao Caiyun had only lived with him for thirty days and had defrauded him of more than 1,700 yuan, this is what is called

"releasing white doves." The facts are clear. In addition to submitting evidence to the court, the plaintiff sues your court, requesting that the defendants be arrested and brought to justice, and punished according to Article 363 of the Criminal Law. He also demands that Yao Caiyun return to cohabit with him, or else requests compensation of 1,400 yuan, as well as clothing and miscellaneous items worth more than 300 yuan." The court approved the complaint, issued summonses, and dispatched constable Guo Xiangyao of the Chinese constabulary to deliver them. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhan Liangce presided over the interrogation in the Fifth Criminal Court. All four defendants were arrested, and lawyers Jiang Yiping and Wu Baotai were hired to defend them. The plaintiff, Shih Hui-hsin, testified that he was 41 years old, from Ningbo, and engaged in the copper and iron business. "Because my elder brother had no son and died years ago, and I only have one son, I wanted to take a concubine. I told people to

pay attention and look for a woman to continue the line of succession. In September of last year, my friend Yuan Jinchun brought a photo of a woman, saying that she was from Wuxi, named Yao Caiyun, and her parents were willing to have her become a concubine. So he set a date for a meeting. On October 26th, Yuan Jinchun, Hua Juquan, and Yao Bochun and his wife brought Caiyun to a hotel room. I went and considered her qualified. The defendants initially asked for a tea ceremony gift of 2,000 yuan, but I only agreed to 700 yuan. Later, we settled on 1,000 yuan. Yao Bochun and his wife then issued a written agreement, and the introducer signed it. I paid 1,000 yuan and took Yao back

to the rented house and lived with her for only thirty-nine days. On December 9th, Yao Bochun and his wife came to my house and said that because of the 'full moon' [one month after the wedding], they needed to take Caiyun back to stay temporarily. I thought this was customary, so I agreed. Unexpectedly, on January 7th, I suddenly received a letter from lawyer Jiang Yiping, saying that he represented Yao Caiyun and demanded to end the relationship with me. But I usually treated Caiyun very well. White fungus and other tonics were always available. Now she suddenly wants to leave, I don't know why. There is a 'releasing white doves' scheme to defraud me of money. Therefore, I filed a lawsuit, demanding that she be ordered to

compensate for the tea ceremony gift and other items, totaling 1,700 yuan." Under questioning, Yao Caiyun testified, "I was indeed married to Shih as a concubine by my parents. But at that time, I was only seventeen years old and my body was not fully developed. Therefore, it was agreed that we should not have sexual relations immediately after I entered his household, but wait two years and I should go to school. But after I entered his household, Shih did not abide by the agreement. On October 8th, he forced me to have sexual relations, causing injury to my lower body, and the pain was unbearable. I sent a letter to my mother to come to Shanghai and accompany me to Dr. Long Zhang's clinic for treatment. He confirmed that I had been injured and said that I could not have sexual relations for 120 days. After half a month of treatment, the injury improved slightly, and my mother returned home. But Shih's

lust arose again. On November 6th, he tried to force me to have sexual relations for the second time. I refused, and Shih used his fingers to dig into me, causing another injury. I was bedridden for several days, suffering greatly. Shih instructed the matchmaker to send a letter to my parents in Shanghai to reason with Shih, but it was ineffective. Therefore, I entrusted lawyer Jiang Yiping to send a letter to question him. Shih disregards human decency and forces sexual relations. Moreover, his treatment is very poor. Therefore, I am unwilling to go back with Shih." Yao Bochun and his wife also gave a testimony, which was largely the same as Caiyun's, but claimed that Shih was 46 years old, had three sons, two of whom were married. They acknowledged receiving 1,000 yuan for the tea ceremony gift, but denied

the 400 yuan in savings and clothing, etc. Witness Yuan Jinchun testified that he was a foreman in the warehouse of Jin Cheng Bank and a friend of Shih. Last year, Shih wanted to take a concubine and asked me to keep an eye out. One day, Hua Juquan invited me to a mahjong game and gave me a photo of a woman to look at, saying that he wanted to betroth her to me. I took it back to Shih to look at, and he found it suitable. So I entrusted Hua to send a letter to Wuxi, inviting Yao Bochun and his wife to come to Shanghai with Caiyun. We agreed on a tea ceremony gift of 1,000 yuan in the hotel, and then she entered his household. I don't know about the rest. Hua Juquan gave a testimony, and then the lawyers for both sides stood up to debate for a long time. Judge Zhan announced that the debate on this case was over and that the verdict would be announced on the 17th of this month.

Regarding this, our Association, standing as a third party, should handle this matter. We ask all comrades to express their opinions." Chen Yiyan, Gu Bingyuan, Hu Xiwei, Lin Chao, Xu Baohua, and others successively expressed their opinions. The Secretariat presented a joint letter from 45 factories, requesting a temporary motion. Chairman Wang retreated from his position due to business, and Chen Yiyan was elected as Chairman. The Chairman summarized the opinions of the majority and proposed three motions, requesting a vote: (1) Goods that are not purely sold under the trademark of national goods should not be certified as national goods. The Desiling bulb should be jointly investigated by representatives from the Association and the Electrical Manufacturing Association. The deadline for reporting to the meeting is next Monday, and a decision will be made. (2) The name of the manufacturing factory should be clearly indicated on the Desiling bulb, and the manufacturer should guarantee it before it can be certified. This was unanimously approved. It was also decided to hand over the first motion to the executive committees of the two associations for handling. It was already 6 o'clock, and the meeting was adjourned with a bell.

Cigarette Exchange Association Reorganizes Market Prices 161

Since the January 28th Incident, the business of the cigarette exchange industry association in this city has been declining day by day. Recently, competition has intensified, and the selling prices of various cigarettes have been disrupted by cheap prices, which has harmed the overall business. Many fellow traders have lost their capital. The association believes that this situation is not beneficial to the industry in the long run. On the 7th of this month, it convened executive supervisors and representatives from wholesale companies throughout the city to discuss together. As a result of the meeting, all industry operators must join the association and obtain a certificate. Those operating in the market must pay an additional market fee. When issuing cigarettes from cigarette companies or wholesale cigarettes from cigarette shops, they must have a certificate of association to prove it, and keep detailed records of the number in the cigarette issuance books and cigarette wholesale books to prevent disorder. Otherwise, the price will be considered that of an individual customer. The Committee for Reorganizing Market Prices, in addition to the executive supervisors as ex officio members, also elected 15 other members to take special responsibility. Several draft proposals were passed, and it was decided to hold another meeting at the association hall at No. 487 Ningbo Road at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month. At that time, each cigarette company will also be asked to send responsible representatives to attend and discuss, cooperate, and decide on various methods. A formal document will be submitted to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs and various courts for filing, and a notice will be requested to be issued. If there is any violation of the execution, it will be strictly prohibited. The general purpose is to benefit the industry, maintain capital, and maintain business.

Reader's Advisor

Going into Monkhood and Returning to Lay Life丨Letter from Ms. Jiang Xin丨 164

I am a half-monastic single woman. When I was five or six years old, my mother died, and my father sent me to a monastic woman with hair to be her apprentice, and I went to a dilapidated temple to become a monk. At that time, I was ignorant and followed my so-called master to chant scriptures every day, but I didn't understand at all what the scriptures said. When I grew to be more than ten years old, my master left all the affairs of the temple to me. All the begging for rice, fundraising, receiving guests, running errands, and everything else, internal and external, was all done by me alone, from morning to night, and I was endlessly busy. My so-called master was just muddleheaded and enjoyed the fruits of my labor. She saw that I was lively, hardworking, and able to endure hardship, and she was very pleased, so she tried every means to win me over, so that I would loyally serve her. But she was still afraid that I would not be a beast of burden for the rest of my life, so not long after, she took in an apprentice for me, and said more nice words to appease my heart. From the outside, it seemed that she was very kind to me, but she didn't like my father and brothers very much, and she rarely favored my relatives and friends who were kind to me. When I was over twenty years old, in those ten years or so, through my personal hard work (which was actually the result of deception), I created everything: the dilapidated temple was renovated by me and looked brand new; the peeling Buddha statues were sculpted by me and shone with gold. I had long realized that the reason why a person becomes a monk is nothing more than that they have bad luck in the middle of their life and are forced to do so. If they really want to practice Zen and enlightenment, they must be able to be clean and quiet. How can I be a true monk with such hard work? Moreover, with such hard work and effort, would I not be able to obtain a good position in society? So why should I bury my useful body in an inexplicable place, living an inhuman life, and ending my days as an outcast? Therefore, I resolved that after completing the two tasks of renovating the temple and sculpting the statues, fulfilling my little wish, I would then return to lay life and restore my original freedom. But my master used every means to control me and refused to let me go, still wanting to use me as her lifelong beast of burden, so that I could never turn over! She already knows my thoughts. She also knows that her tricks of hypocrisy and righteousness are ultimately not enough to trap me, so she uses threats, threatening to die. According to what she told people, if I ran away on my own, she would say that I had run away with someone, report it to the authorities for arrest, and if they couldn't catch me, she would say that my father and brothers had tempted and hidden me, stirring up trouble, and she would sue my father and brothers. In this way, I would have no way to escape her trap. Sir, I am a woman, weak and ignorant. How can I withstand such threats? Therefore, I am raising the following questions and hoping that you can teach me: (1) Are monks beneficial to the country and society, or are they harmful to the country and society? (2) Is it a dishonorable thing for a monk to return to lay life? (3) Does a monk need to obtain the master's consent before returning to lay life, or can they act freely? (4) Is there any legal relationship between master and apprentice? (5) If a master does not want an apprentice to return to lay life and therefore seeks death, should the apprentice bear legal responsibility? (6) If one returns to lay life without the master's permission, is it considered a private escape? Should one be legally bound for fleeing because one does not want to be a monk? (7) After I freely return to lay life, can the master demand my return from my father and brothers? (Reply to be published tomorrow)

Education News Highlights

Ministry of Education Discusses Regulations for Normal Schools 165

Regulations on the Powers and Responsibilities of Primary and Secondary Schools to be Promulgated Simultaneously After the Legislative Yuan passed the Normal School Law and the Primary and Secondary School Law, the Ministry of Education had already drafted regulations for primary and secondary schools and regulations for vocational schools. These have been passed by the ministry's meetings in phases and are being sorted out and finalized. The regulations for normal schools were discussed at the ministry's meeting on the 9th and 10th of this month. Vice Ministers, Directors, Secretaries, Councilors, Supervisors, Section Chiefs, etc. all attended the discussion. A total of more than 130 regulations, one-third were passed on the 9th, and the general outline was passed on the 10th. After further sorting out, they will be promulgated simultaneously with the regulations for middle schools, primary schools, and vocational schools. It is heard that the Normal School Law passed by the Legislative Yuan previously did not address the status of rural teachers. There are currently more than 550 rural normal schools across the country. The Ministry of Education, based on the requests of rural teachers in various provinces, has provided considerable relief in the drafting of normal school regulations. This discussion held that in order to promote universal education, as Chinese villagers account for 70-80% of the population, normal schools, in addition to those located in cities, should be established in rural areas. Normal schools that are specifically designed to train rural primary school teachers may also be called rural normal schools. The entire regulations are relatively concrete and adaptable to the organization of normal schools and all necessary conditions.

Remarks by Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Education, on "Education in Shanghai" (Part 4) 171

Overview of School Education and Social Education

Firstly, due to the large number of illiterate people in society, which is the biggest obstacle to all new construction in China, before the implementation of universal compulsory education, we must first start with "establishing more public schools" to achieve the first step of "compulsory education for the common people." Here, we can compare the number of public schools established in the first session six years ago with the number of public schools established this year.

First Session: 20 schools, 354 graduates

Seventh Session: 54 schools, 1453 graduates

From this, we can see the efforts made since the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government. The number of schools has increased nearly threefold, and the number of graduates has increased more than fourfold. We believe that in a few years, these public schools will have even greater development, and the suffering of illiterate people and the reduction of many social ills caused by "the causes of illiteracy" will make us very optimistic about the future of overall social construction.

In addition, in order to enable some merchants and workers to gain knowledge after work, several supplementary schools have been established, which are also completely free. These supplementary schools also have a history of five years. The first session only opened four schools, but now it has expanded to nineteen schools. The number of students has also increased from forty to four hundred and fifty.

From the annual increase in the number of schools and students, it is clear that we attach importance to social education and the effective response we have received from implementing social education.

Secondly, in addition to establishing free public schools and supplementary schools, the Municipal Bureau of Education also has the following facilities for the implementation of social education:

㈠ Public Education Center: It has fixed activities such as "popular lectures," "academic lectures," "public entertainment," "museum exhibitions," and "reading of books and newspapers." In addition, various gatherings related to social activities are held from time to time, such as "public hiking meetings," "speech contests," etc.

㈡ Library: Currently, there is only one municipal library, which was established only one year ago, so the content is not very rich. However, all architectural equipment has been carefully designed, and there are already established steps for expansion plans. It is expected that there will be rapid development within five years.

㈢ Mobile Library: This mobile library is very convenient for the general public, because the public in this city can borrow books from the library to read, the procedures are very simple, and there is no charge.

㈣ Zoo: The zoo is newly established, so the content is not very rich. However, it has already aroused considerable interest among the general public.

㈤ Public School Gardens: These public school gardens are provided to help students study natural sciences. All common plants in natural science textbooks are available. Not only can students get the convenience of self-study and appreciation in natural sciences, but also provide a place for some citizens to relax and enjoy themselves after work.

㈥ Public Sports Field: Promoting physical education is a task that the education authorities pay close attention to. Therefore, the equipment of public sports fields is also expanding day by day. We can only use the number of people exercising in public sports fields as evidence to know the strong interest of the citizens in physical education and the greatness of its inevitable effect. At the same time, because there is only one public sports field and the area of this city is very vast, six simple public sports fields have been established in various districts so that the public scattered in various districts have places to exercise and engage in sports. In the future, some more of these simple sports fields will be added to make physical education the most common training.

The above-mentioned social education facilities are all managed by the Municipal Bureau of Education. In addition, there are many public schools and cultural institutions privately established by the public in this city, which can help the government's social education facilities. According to the latest statistics, the following are available:

Libraries 12 Vocational Training Institutes 5 Supplementary Schools 17

Cultural and Educational Groups 44 Correspondence Schools 3 Special Schools (Deaf and Mute Education)

Total 82

In addition, we believe that social education has a special meaning for "public entertainment," so we pay extreme attention to public entertainment at the same time.

Western United Football Group A

Invincible and Unbeatable, Donghua Defeats British Navy 181

Eight to One, Four Goals in Each Half

Navy Relied on Free Kick, Not Completely Defeated

Flustered and Flustered, the Whole Field Burst into Laughter

The Donghua Football Team, invincible and unbeatable, defeated the British Navy 8-1 at Recreation Ground yesterday. The first half was 4-1. This is Donghua's thirteenth victory in Group A. From now on, the championship is near, and there is no problem with nineteen. Only two games against the Western Capture Argyll remain. The British Navy was represented by the Suffolk ship yesterday. All members of the team, except for two selected from the gunboat, were members of the ship. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

Donghua Team 182

The Whole Field Laughed 184

It has been a long time since we saw good football, and the continuous cloudy and rainy days combined with snow. Yesterday, it suddenly cleared up. In addition, the Western United Football Association's announcement made the Recreation Ground very crowded with guests, around three to four thousand. It was thought that there might be some outstanding players in the navy, but I did not know that they were still depressed. The forwards were okay, but the defenders were not good. The left winger Du Lie Lan was the most outstanding of the forwards. He made several passes, which were fast and accurate, and were worth watching. The weakness of the defenders, when the Donghua forwards attacked, made them flustered and at a loss. For a time, the whole field suddenly burst into laughter.

Back and Forth 185

In the first half, the navy took the offensive. Although the progress was not fast, the attack was fierce. They often hovered around the Donghua field. The wingers had occasional long shots. Seven minutes after the start of the game, Donghua broke through the navy. Li Yichen made a long pass from the right corner. Chen Yutian rushed in like a fly. The navy quickly started to chase back. Yutian had reached 15 yards from the enemy's goal. He calmly flew into the net. Donghua won 1-0. Yutian got another chance to break through, but failed. The navy was still attacking fiercely. Du Lie Lan's central pass was almost headed in. Li Yichen suddenly touched the ball with his hand 25 yards in front of the goal. Brown kicked a free kick, which was as fast as an arrow. It hit the right post and bounced into the goal. 1-1, each scored a goal. Courtesy demands reciprocity.

Header Skills 186

At this time, the situation was still tense. Donghua gradually saw the offensive, but the repeated long shots did not score. At 20 minutes, Li Yichen passed to Chen Yutian. Chen got the ball and went straight forward. He kicked the ball flat in front of the goal from the corner. Li Yichen saw the opportunity in front of him. He could not kick it, so he jumped up and headed the ball right in the middle. The ball went into the goal, and Li fell straight in front of the goal. Applause rang out. In less than three minutes, Wan Xianghua got a pass from Li Yichen, broke through two barriers in a row, and shot diagonally towards the goal, and it went into the net again. Donghua won 3-1.

Center Back Colors 187

There were still 25 minutes left in the first half. Feng Yunyou, the center back, also went forward to assist the attack and also scored a goal. Ministry of Education Orders Students to Attend Summer Physical Education Training Classes 198

(Nanjing, 11th) The Ministry of Education has decided to run summer physical education training classes in Beijing from July 10th to August 20th. Physical education teachers in primary and secondary schools and those who have considerable research and interest in physical education will be admitted to receive further training to meet the current urgent needs. The regulations and budget have been approved by the Executive Yuan, and all preparatory committees are actively preparing to start school on schedule. (Nanjing, 11th) The physical education training class will accept current physical education teachers in primary and secondary schools, staff members of physical education venues, teachers of martial arts halls, or those who have considerable research and interest in physical education to receive further training. On the 11th, all education departments and bureaus were ordered to send in the academic qualifications and experiences of each student before May 1st for review by the preparatory committee. After receiving the qualification notification, they will then be instructed to attend school. The number of students in the class is tentatively set at 100.

Observing the history and achievements of the Liangjiang basketball team, it is clear that they do not suffer from the ailment of empty talk without action. They simply put in the effort practically, doing what they say, constantly working diligently and moving forward. Although they defeated Japan twenty years ago, they show no signs of complacency, remaining humble and eager to learn from the sports of other countries in Europe and America, integrating their essence to create independent and outstanding sports. This kind of grand ambition, far-reaching vision, and arduous work, they are willing to dedicate years to, traveling across oceans to accomplish. It is truly admirable.

Their declaration states that considerations of victory or defeat are not their primary concern. Although these are words of humility, we cannot judge the value of their trip based on their success or failure, or on our own pessimistic speculations. Their trip abroad comes at a time when the nation faces numerous challenges, and the world is observing the survival capabilities of the Chinese nation after our revolution. This trip can and should provide foreigners with some new stimulation, changing their perceptions of our nation. Their ambition is commendable, and their intentions are virtuous. It is no different from the heroic spirit of going to the enemy with generosity and sacrifice. As the elders say, establishing the beginning of self-strengthening as pioneers for men, truly demonstrates its significance.

Furthermore, since the school began preparations and implementation, the Chinese people have also changed their past negative attitude of criticizing others' work, instead providing active and practical assistance. The public opinion following the disclosure of this news in various newspapers has been consistently enthusiastic and encouraging. Therefore, I dare to predict that the Chinese people will definitely help them succeed. Moreover, I hope the Liangjiang basketball team will strive diligently and live up to the hopes of the nation.
