Free Talk

Vagrant (II) 201

— Zhou Jia

Wandering, wandering, I don't know how far I wandered, and I ended up stumbling into a small vegetable market. Wow! The vegetable market was really crowded! The women, a bunch here, a group there, arguing with the vegetable vendors over greens, tofu, and gluten, elbows bumping into baskets, baskets bumping into scales, it was a real mess. I squeezed in, taking every opportunity to stretch out my five fingers, pinching this, fondling that, it was quite enjoyable. But that couldn't satisfy my hunger! Just as I was hesitating, thinking about sneaking away to another place to find food, I suddenly ran into two fellow gamblers, setting up a game of chance right there, "guessing the coffin."

Heh! These two guys are really something! They actually came here to do business. How come I didn't think of that? All those women are greedy for small gains, as long as you set the hook, you're not afraid of not catching a fish. But where are the patrolmen? I looked for a long time but couldn't find any. Could it be that these two guys have such incredible courage that they aren't afraid of the cops or the street vendors, so they came out to do business? I quietly walked up, and gently called out to the dealer:

"Li Si, you little rascal."

Li Si turned around, saw me, and quickly gave me a wink, reaching back with his arm, giving me two small silver coins. I knew he wanted me to help him attract customers. Fine! I'll help you attract customers, and then you'll have to share with me. I bet on three, and a three came up, I bet on four, and a four came up. Betting back and forth like this, I almost took all the small silver coins in Li Si's hand. A large crowd of women gathered around to watch the excitement.

One woman gave me a small silver coin, wanting me to bet with her. As soon as I took it, I performed a magic trick, turning one coin into two. Heh! This fish is hooked! The woman's eyes were really small, getting two small silver coins, she smiled from ear to ear and started betting herself, not needing my help anymore. Good! I'll watch you bet. Bet on three, get a four; bet on four, get a three. In short, the three of us, working together, took all the grocery money from many women's pockets, then packed up our tools, leaving those women standing there dumbfounded, their eyes red with anger.

Li Si's conscience wasn't bad. After the game, in a dark alley, he divided eight small silver coins to me. It's been a long time since I've had so much money. I'm really lucky today, wherever I go, I make a profit! These past two days, I've been eating nothing but potstickers, my mouth is starting to taste bland. Today, I have to change my taste. I immediately rushed into a Yangchun noodle restaurant, ordered a bowl of noodles with extra broth, and ate and drank to my heart's content.

But, ill-gotten gains come quickly and go quickly. As soon as I ran out of the noodle restaurant, I ran into a few young men selling sesame twists and salted peanuts, clanging their copper coins on the steps at the corner of a doorway. As soon as I saw that, my heart started to flutter, and I joined in. Clanging the copper coins for three hours, I lost two small silver coins; plus, I bought a few puffs of opium and a few pieces of dried tobacco, and my eight small silver coins were reduced to five.

If I use these five small silver coins carefully, I can definitely use them for ten days or so. I tucked them tightly into my inner pocket. Today, I don't want to gamble anymore. (To be continued)

Monster and Beast Movies 202

— Xuan

According to statistics from the Mainland Press, the best-selling films in Shanghai last year were "Same Heart Knot," "Tarzan the Ape Man," "A History of the Red Chamber," "Frankenstein," "Dragon and Tiger Fight," and other five films. It is remembered that the opening of "Paradise for Women" at the Nanjing Grand Theater on New Year's Day this year sold out even the tickets for the second showing one hour before the first showing. "Tarzan the Ape Man," "Frankenstein," "Dragon and Tiger Fight," and "Paradise for Barbarian Women" are all so-called monster, barbarian, and beast movies, which are not realistic life themes. This kind of non-realistic life monster, barbarian, and beast films (and even novels) were popular in Europe and America two years ago, and have not declined to this day, and Shanghai has also been affected.

The meaning is that the general public desires to "escape reality!"

Why escape reality? Because in this cruel and competitive society, they feel there is no way out; because this declining capitalist society is already "spiritually bankrupt," as many fascist scholars in Europe have painfully confessed. From the escape from reality, we see the decadence, confusion, and pessimism of the declining class. This is their subconscious revelation!

On the other hand, because movies are a universal art for the masses, the ruling class must take advantage of it. They have tried to deceive the public on the screen, such as the many "ideal future world" films released in 1929-30 (one of which is "Metropolis," the Chinese translation seems to be "Scientific World"); they have also tried to "prepare consciousness" for the Second World War, such as the endless "martial" war films in recent years. In addition to these two, they also cleverly "avoid reality" and guide the eyes of the general public to monsters, beasts, and barbarians. This is to anesthetize the audience!

Just because one party intentionally wants to avoid reality, and the other party, the general public, subconsciously wants to escape reality, then monster, beast, and barbarian films sell extremely well!

However, it is precisely on this point that we see the world's ruling class frantically and the confusion, hesitation, decadence, and pessimism of the general public under their "education."

The Strange Custom of Widow Suicide in India 203

— Wan Ju

Widow suicide is a product of the strange concept of chastity of Indians, and it can also be said to be a characteristic of Indian civilization. I don't know when this matter started. We can't find this rule in the Vedas, which shows that there was no such cruel custom in ancient India. However, there is such a record in "Puranas" (ancient history of India): "A widow who can ascend the cremation altar with her husband's remains is a chaste woman, and she can enter heaven after death. If a widow survives after her husband's death, especially if she remarries, then she will not be qualified to follow her husband in the next life." Because of this absurd legend, this inhumane custom occurred. Although many people in modern times have criticized this bad custom, Indian widows, even if they do not commit suicide, dare not remarry; although there are occasional exceptions, they are rare. On December 4, 1829, Indian Governor-General William. Mettingk promulgated a law that absolutely prohibits the burning of widows, and violators will be sentenced to death. However, when this law was implemented, it unexpectedly encountered major obstacles: generally ignorant women, seduced by monks and religious superstitions, shouted loudly that they were willing to be burned to death to be martyred for their husbands: Therefore, the authorities had to let them act freely. If the government really adopted tough prohibition measures, it might cause serious chaos. Fortunately, later, the relatives of the widow issued a statement stating that they did not insist on burning the widow, so the authorities reiterated the ban, and this custom in British India gradually disappeared. However, after the 1860 rebellion, the Olts area openly burned widows again, and as a result, the perpetrators were sentenced to death; in 1875, this inhumane act occurred in the Laknu area, and the court prosecuted 30 people involved for murder and sentenced them to death. After that, this custom was no longer seen in British India, but in the native princes’ countries, there was no way to stop it.

When the burning ceremony is about to be held, many people from far and near gather spontaneously to watch this sacrificial ceremony. The widow is dressed in gorgeous clothes like a bride, supported by her close relatives, and monks and religious superstitious people surround her. The unfortunate widow is led to the cremation ground in the interweaving of music. The road from home to the cremation ground is paved with leaves, bouquets and palm trees. If the widow who is about to commit suicide is still energetic, she will throw money to the beggars on the side of the road while walking, but most of the widows at that time are completely unconscious; because before the suicide is carried out, people often drink a kind of anesthetic made of Indian cannabis.

In that extremely tragic silence, the crowd surrounded the cremation altar. The widow slowly circled the altar three times, then the monk

Long Creative Work

Crossroads of the Times and Love (Continued Draft) 204

— Zhang Ping

She embraced him and went up the stairs from the second floor. He also followed the momentum and stepped onto the stairs. When he came to his room, he noticed that she was only wearing a velvet white pajamas, a large area of her snowy white chest was exposed, and she was wearing a pair of short floral pants underneath. Her entire calf below the knees was exposed.

"What a moving pose!"

He forgot the current predicament again, and only indulged in admiring her semi-naked posture like a glutton.

"Oh my! How embarrassing!"

She laughed, covered her face with both palms, and turned around like a little girl, running downstairs.

After seeing her leave, his mind gradually calmed down. He felt that his actions just now were too reckless. Apologize to them? A dignified Chinese citizen can't do that. I would rather defend the land to the death than lose an inch of land from my hands! But staying here is not a good idea strategically. Who can predict how this predicament will unfold?

"Thirty-six strategies, running away is the best strategy!"

Thinking of this, he hurriedly put on his shoes and socks, then buttoned up his coat. He couldn't pack anything, so he only took his necessary wallet, toothbrush, and towel, and rushed downstairs. Fortunately, he didn't run into Mrs. Tsuruko on the way, nor did he see the maid. He walked out of the alley entrance and suddenly saw the beautiful girl who came with that Japanese guy, still wearing gorgeous Japanese clothes, holding four brick-shaped breads in her hand, walking from the other side. When she saw Haiquan, she smiled and bowed to him.

"This is really an angel descended from heaven!"

He felt a lot of shameful contradictions, but he couldn't help but return a salute. He hurried to the tram stop.

"That old guy is her father, then that little girl is her sister, right, that's definitely right."

Thinking this, he was ashamed again, his whole mind was still dominated by her. He couldn't help but sigh again.

The priest then helped her onto the place where her husband's body was placed. At a distance of a few steps from the body, she was made to sit cross-legged; sometimes the dead person's head was placed on the widow's lap. Then she was tied to the firewood pile on the cremation altar. Some people poured oil as much as possible, and some hurriedly lit the fire. After the fire was lit, the monks recited scriptures and sang hymns loudly, and relatives began to cry, and trumpets and drums were played all around. This disturbance could prevent the tragic cries from being heard. If the widow was burned and in pain, broke the rope, and jumped out of the raging fire to escape, the cruel monks would rush to catch her and throw her back into the fire.

If a widow has an attempt to avoid her own tragic fate, the monks and her relatives will consider it an ominous sign, the most unlucky thing, and the soul of the dead will not become a Buddha. Sometimes, for fear that the widow would resist, when she climbed onto the cremation altar, people also used a large and heavy bamboo pole to press on her shoulders, making it impossible for her to stand up.

When the cremation altar was still slightly burning, the crowd dispersed silently. Usually, the widow's body was not completely burned. The relatives cleaned up the altar and remains and buried them together.

Although this tragic and cruel custom stems from religious superstition, the concept of husband and wife as one is also an important factor!

Suzhou People 205

— Ms. Peng Xuezhen

I really don't understand why I hate Suzhou so much, although I have been living in this world all the time.

I like majesty, and I like the atmosphere of those straightforward people. In Suzhou, I was disappointed. Everything pays attention to beauty, people are like sugar figurines, sticky and lively, blood is out of the question, the average people are as leisurely as stagnant water, motionless, as if there is no source of life. Suzhou people are particularly strong in their housekeeping, and those who have a little food don't want to run outside. For the sake of a comfortable life, many people from other provinces have come to live in Suzhou in recent years.

In Suzhou, there are particularly many unemployed young masters, and they can spend the long days without any effort. Teahouses and hotels are booming, probably for this reason. When you have nothing to do, buy some calligraphy and paintings to play with, invite someone to play a tune, and act as an amateur; smoke and gambling also embellish this leisurely life. Suzhou women are also almost the same as modern girls, with a bit of the atmosphere of Lin Daiyu in the 20th century.

Except for the few existing roads, most of the roads are paved with stones, and it hurts to walk a long way; on drizzly days, that slippery feeling is really good, but this is only known to people who walk on foot.

Around eight o'clock in the morning, it is the time for young masters and young ladies to take a car to school丨of course, there are also those who do not take a car. The crossroads are full of rickshaw drivers waiting to do business.

The stove door is especially busy in the early morning, and the girls and mothers-in-law who soak water are all standing full, waiting and chatting, and those who arrive first carry the full water bottle and wander back and forth on the street. Children chase each other in front of the door, and half a fried dough stick satisfies everything, always grinning. Children who can't walk stand at the doorway, gazing at the corner of the wall, with two snot hanging from the corners of their lips.

Suzhou people are really too leisurely, even the servants and children show a leisurely appearance. They all seem to be dreaming, lingering in a dream. Ah, when will the torrent of the times awaken these leisurely Suzhou people who are dreaming all day long!

Financial News: Gold Market Rises Uninterruptedly Over the Past Week 206

Yesterday Rose Another 9.6 Candareens, Totaling a Rise of 16.1 Taels Over Six Days

(Overview) Yesterday, according to foreign dispatches, London's spot and forward gold prices remained unchanged. New York silver prices also showed no increase or decrease. Exchange rates slightly decreased, with forward silver prices down only a slight 0.8 candareens. American cotton continued to rise, increasing from 2 to 6 pounds. The gold market should have slightly declined. Although the opening price was 803 taels, the foreign exchange market also opened without clear gains or losses. Retail investors were still sellers, so the gold price first fell to 802 taels and 4 candareens. Afterwards, due to Citibank entering this month's US dollars at 8 yuan, and major players continuing to drag on transactions, prices trended higher, reaching 805 taels and 8 candareens. Later, the upward trend stopped. As the trend stabilized, retail investors took advantage of the high price to sell, causing a slight pullback. Additionally, foreign dispatches indicated that India might cancel the increased silver import tax, further dropping the price to 803 taels and 4 candareens. However, market confidence remained stable, and buyers continued to flood in, allowing the gold price to be maintained. It fluctuated around 4 taels before closing at 804 taels and 4 candareens. In the afternoon, the market was closed due to Saturday. The market situation during the half-day was stable, and there were no disturbances. The 'cooked red' (shredded gold) price had risen to around 13 taels above the standard price. Swap spreads were also high, ranging from 3.5 to 5 taels. The Central Bank had already intervened to regulate the market, buying in at 5 taels, and then selling off. Spot market openings were also few. It was rumored that Hengxing had brokered 105 bars at a price of 4 taels. The half-day market situation is recorded below.

(Morning Session) The morning opened at 803 taels, a slight decrease of 5 candareens from the previous close, but not significant. Merchandise spot trading had reached 0.12 taels, bolstering market confidence, leading to a pullback. Merchandise opened at 802 taels and 7 candareens. The foreign exchange market also opened stable, with the near-term British exchange rate quoted at 1 shilling, 7 pence, and 625 points, and the US exchange rate at 8 yuan, showing a slight decrease to 2 taels and 4 candareens. Major players continued to absorb supply. Hengyu took the lead, buying up to 4 taels. Merchandise was also purchased at 4.5 taels. Citibank bought this month's US dollars at 8 yuan. Fuyu came up and dragged in transactions, reaching 5 taels. Yuanchun and Hengyu continued to buy up to 5.5 taels. Dadecheng slightly sold, retreating to 4 taels and 8 candareens. Yuanmaoyong and Runchangyong both bought in, pushing the price up to 805 taels and 8 candareens. At this point, retail investors rushed to sell. Foreign dispatches indicated that India might cancel the increased silver import tax, leading to a downstream movement. Citibank sold March US dollars at 8 yuan, and Hongli also sold, dropping to around 4 taels. Yuanmaoyong bought again, raising the price by several candareens. The Progress of New US Cotton is Affected by the Climate 222

However, Most News About Cotton Fields May Need To Be Increased 丨 A New York dispatch on the 10th reported on the cotton market during the week, stating that at the beginning of last week, a storm occurred at the Gibbon Bank in New Orleans, which caused long positions to be liquidated and further accelerated. However, the storm at the bank passed peacefully afterwards, so short covering and re-buying followed. The demand for cotton cloth was better, and the news about farmland relief from Washington was also good, so buying interest was also encouraged. Recently, the climate has been quite unfavorable for the arrangement of farmland and the sale of primary cotton fertilizer. In the 13 southern states, January increased by 20% compared to the same period last year. Some experts believe that the low temperature in the western cotton belt is sufficient to restrain the larvae of boll weevils. The clearing of cotton fields has generally increased. However, this view still depends on the future market conditions and the agricultural crop production debt rules announced by the Ministry of Agriculture.

Business Tips (8)

Selecting Wood Ear: Thin Slices, Large Fruiting Bodies, Low Price 229

"Wood ear" is a type of fungus, cool in nature, produced in Sichuan and other places. It grows on trees and resembles an ear in shape, hence the name "wood ear." High-grade varieties, such as Sichuan ear, Malanping ear, and Yan ear, have standard characteristics: they are dark and glossy, have large and abundant fruiting bodies, thin slices, light texture, and few impurities. Second-grade varieties, such as HeKou ear, GuCheng ear, YiChang ear, and XingAn ear, are generally similar in quality, but differ in that they have fewer large fruiting bodies, a duller color, or heavier impurities. HeKou ear, in particular, tends to have thicker slices. The lowest grade includes NanZhang ear and YangPing ear, which are characterized by thick and heavy slices, and many impurities. YangPing ear is even more likely to contain mud and sand, making it the lowest quality wood ear.

"Uses": Mostly used as a side dish, but its cool and moisturizing nature can nourish yin. Although not as good as white fungus, regular consumption has similar benefits.

"Preparation": Soak in water until fully rehydrated, remove the edges, and use only the base of the ear. Wash thoroughly and simmer in water until tender, then add rock sugar to taste. This is a unique dish that is comparable to silver fungus.

"Medicinal Use": Charred into ash and ground into a powder, taken with a light salt water solution, it can treat stomach ailments.

Spring and Autumn

The Southward Migration of Culture 253

— Zhan Lu

Beiping, doesn't it bear the honor of being a city of culture? Once the highly anticipated southward migration of cultural relics is implemented, won't the city of culture be merely superficial? Because of this question, waves of opposition are surging. In fact, the southward migration of culture is not something to oppose. I am moved by the southward migration of culture from Beiping to reflect on the lack of a southward migration of military strength from the three northeastern provinces! It's a pity that it didn't happen! To put it elegantly, "Is it the fortune of culture or the misfortune of military strength?"

If the Northeastern authorities had cherished military strength as they cherish culture today, before the September 18th Incident, they would have moved all military-related airplanes, guns, bullets, and equipment to the south in large quantities. That would have increased the anti-Japanese forces during the January 28th Incident, causing greater wounds to the enemy.

Since the military strength of the past did not migrate south, the culture of the present must migrate south as soon as possible. Northern scholars naturally disregard the southward migration of culture, while southern scholars shout slogans of unparalleled glory for the southward migration of culture.

Where does the glory lie? The glory lies in the fact that in this era of "literary works being worthless in times of chaos," society is actually changing its martial habits and becoming right-oriented in spirit! Aren't literary figures about to rise? The military strength of the past was not worth migrating south, but only the culture of Beiping, only the Palace Museum culture of Beiping, is worth migrating. Who says the world is not at peace? Emphasizing literature and de-emphasizing military strength is a symbol of peace! Southern archaeologists, epigraphers, artists, and all gentlemen holding pens will surely enthusiastically shout slogans for the once-in-a-millennium southward migration of culture!

The southward migration of culture is even more glorious than what Song scholars called "the southward journey of our Dao."

International Tycoons 254

— Bai He

| Seeking Opportunities, Taking Advantage

Shanghai has many idle people, tycoons, who loiter on the streets all day long. When they see a country bumpkin wearing nailed shoes and carrying an umbrella, walking along looking around, they immediately size him up. Then, they deliberately bump into the bumpkin. This behavior is called "seeking opportunities" by the tycoons. After "seeking opportunities," they scold, "Stupid pig, didn't bring your eyes (棗子) with you? Why did you bump into me?" Then, they immediately deliver two slaps. As a result, the country bumpkin digs out silver dollars from his pocket to pay his respects to the tycoon, and also has to apologize a hundred and twenty times before the tycoon deigns to spare him, wearing his hat askew and muttering, "Stupid pig, consider yourself lucky, next time be more careful when you walk." The Northeast Incident in our country is just like a country bumpkin meeting a Shanghai tycoon. Look, who exactly blew up the South Manchurian Railway on September 18th? It's obvious, it was "seeking opportunities." Then came the warning, which is clearly like someone bumping into another person and then scolding them, "Stupid pig... Why did you bump into me?" After the warning, military action was launched immediately, without waiting for negotiations, just like the Shanghai tycoon slapping the country bumpkin twice before he could even argue. It's a pity that our China, without a doubt, is acting like a country bumpkin who, after being slapped twice, silently gives up everything in his pocket. It's a pity that we haven't apologized a hundred and twenty times yet, and the tycoon still thinks we're "not being cooperative." Otherwise, the tycoon would have already walked away wearing his hat askew, and perhaps the Battle of Rehe wouldn't have happened.

Soviet Foreign Minister Maxim Litvinov, at the Geneva Disarmament Conference, advocated defining aggression and refuted the various absurd reasons for carrying out aggression in a reasonable and logical manner. His concluding remarks said, "If war is regarded as a way to ensure peace, then there will never be an aggressor in armed conflicts." The country bumpkin listened to these words with great interest. But I wonder, what do the international tycoons think?

The Three Loves Doctrine 255

— Chen Yinong

| The Trilogy of Life |

We all know that our President Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People for saving the country and the people were developed from Lincoln's speech (Of the people, by the people, for the people). Now, I have also derived the Three Loves Doctrine from the English "from love in love with love," which is a true portrayal of life. Its meaning is to be born out of self-love, to live with love, and to die for love. Let me illustrate it below.

This is what the Bible says for sure: After Adam and Eve stole the apple in God's orchard, they understood unprecedented love, and loved everything. Alas, the failure or success of love ultimately comes down to death!

To be born out of self-love, to live with love, and to die for love is called the trilogy of life. Who says it's not appropriate?

A Two-Sided View of Women's Clothing 256

— Long

| A Masterpiece of Pseudo-Moralists |

During my time as a news reporter, there was hardly a day when I didn't go to the Public Security Bureau to investigate social discoveries. What I can't forget the most is the pair of young men and women found near the City God Temple. I am most dissatisfied with the social news that has always flowed into the lower-level vulgar tastes of consciousness, I can not publish it, in my observation, it is really not considered "news."

It was a summer evening: A man was wearing a red and white striped undershirt that reached his belly; below, he wore a pair of white shorts with blue trim, revealing his hairy legs without the protection of woolen socks. It looked like an athlete's outfit. His companion, a young lady, was wearing a red thin silk cheongsam, covered with the most popular new-style coat with a high collar. The two of them walked in shoulder to shoulder from the New North Gate. Who knew that they would immediately be surrounded by hooligans on the street, gathering more and more people, causing bystanders to shout curiously:

"Look! Everyone look, this pair of weirdos..." Then the voices became mixed and loud, and heads floated in the shouts like melons in a field. As a result, due to disrupting public order, the police officers politely asked them to go to the Public Security Bureau. The police chief said to me, "Strange and gaudy clothes promote licentiousness, they deserve it." And he wanted me to publish this matter in the newspaper. I smiled without saying anything. How could I regard this as "news"!

Novel

The Adventures of Mixed-River Dragon 257

— Huo Xueming

The moon is very bright, it is a winter night; there is not a single star, and the celestial body flows with clear blue light.

The old parasol trees, more than ten feet high, lined up on the bank, sparsely covered with a few black and scorched remnant leaves, mocked by the whispering, chilly night wind. Various weeds on the verge of death, lying low at the foot of the trees, also sent out piteous tones like light, secluded sobs. The official road wore a dry face; the soil also cracked; a white strip, like a silver snake, but because of the branches and leaves blown by the wind on it, it painted on its body with a vivid and endless strange riddle-like artistic conception.

In short, it was a winter night that froze the world. The men and women in wealthy families were all chatting around the stove.

Suddenly, a faint shadow swayed on the official road, flitting like a wandering soul, but gradually the shadow deepened and darkened, and the sound of coughing could be heard, but it was very light, followed by the sound of footsteps. The sounds of insects nearby seemed afraid of being discovered; they stopped completely. Here, there were only the sounds of wind and leaves, the sounds of footsteps, and occasionally the dry cough of an old man.

In the moonlight, Mixed-River Dragon Li Si was immediately discovered. His owl-like, shining pair of small eyes were pressed under the brim of his old felt hat, vaguely searching for the way. His neck was shrunk between his two towering shoulder blades, as if afraid of the cold. Yes, thick green snot was clearly flowing under his wine-red nose.

He walked very fast, although it was unusually laborious. The fishing net on his back, the harpoon tightly held in his hand, and the fish basket slung around his waist, made him look like the most savage type of professional in the countryside.

"Damn, that shrew, she's ruined my whole life!" He was fed up, squinting his eyes and spitting out a slight curse. Then he clenched his teeth, breathed out a cold breath, and continued to walk north along the official road. In his mind, he imagined the memories of his wife having an affair with someone else, repeatedly quarreling with him, and then running away. (I)

Plant the seeds of love, and when the melons are ripe and fall, a group of human children and grandchildren will be produced. In other words, the source of mankind is the crystallization of their love.

Since we planted the roots of love before we were born, we will naturally not be able to jump out of the hands of the god of love after we become adults. Therefore, as soon as men and women reach the age of sixteen or seventeen, they will understand what love is without being taught, and they will also be very good at practicing it, and they will even shout "Sweetheart" "Dear" Thus, love heaven and love earth, living in the hands of the god of love,

If love succeeds, what will happen? Of course, they will be happy to death! If love fails, what will happen? Of course, their hearts will ache to death! Therefore, they either swallow sleeping pills or jump into the Huangpu River to seek relief.

The True Face of Famous Woman Zhang Guoyun 258

Tomorrow I appreciated a basketball game between a boys' middle school and a girls' normal school on the basketball court. On both sides of the grid, blue and black vests were jumping, and red and white shorts were also active. The arms and fat legs of the men and women naturally danced so naked, attracting the attention of tens of thousands of eyes. However, the costumes of the players on this ball court are more dazzling and more gorgeous than the lovers found in the City God Temple; by analogy, it seems that moralists should scold "hindering public morals." But in the end, I have not seen an order from the Public Security Bureau prohibiting ball games.

Ordinary women are said to be seductive when they bare their legs and wrists, while female athletes are praised for "showing physical health." In fact, these contradictions are just errors in the understanding of pseudo-moralists.

Children's Paradise

The Hungry Eagle 259

— Bing Yu

In ancient times, there was a pair of pigs lying side by side in the wilderness near a village. An old eagle flew from the sky. The eagle's stomach was very hungry, and seeing two fat pigs below, it wanted to seize them in one fell swoop. He soared in the air for a while, suddenly opened his claws and looked down, grabbing fiercely at the backs of the two pigs. His left claw pierced into the back flesh of the male pig, and his right claw pierced into the back flesh of the female pig. The two pigs were both awakened and felt extremely painful on their backs, and they ran wildly and rampaged desperately. At this time, the eagle's two claws were both pierced into the backs of the two pigs and could not be pulled out, so it was split in two at the feet by the two pigs and died. Therefore, there is an old saying from ancient times: "The hungry eagle died with its legs split," which is used to compare the meaning of dying because of excessive greed. There are indeed many people in today's society who are as greedy as hungry eagles, resulting in their deaths!

A Word About Goldfish 261

— Miao Shen

Goldfish are the kind of fish that are good to look at but not good to eat. In Lanxi, Zhejiang, there is a story about goldfish: It is said that there used to be a family with only a mother and daughter, lonely and helpless, struggling to make a living. The daughter was born very filial, and went out to do some small business every day, earning some meager interest to support her old mother; but she herself was often hungry because her income was not enough for the two of them to eat, and she did not dare to tell her mother. Once in winter, just as heavy snow was falling, she went out to do her business as usual, braving the snow, but she knew that she had shouted all day and there was not a single customer. For several days in a row, the old mother groaned in bed with hunger, and she was so anxious that she just cried. She had a subconscious impulse, begging for the compassion of Heaven, and she also thought about going to the stream behind her house to catch a few fish to fill her stomach. She cried sadly, dripping bright red tears, and staggered to the stream behind her house. But she knew that at this time her filial piety had moved Heaven, and countless golden little fish fell into the stream. When she arrived at the stream, she saw schools of fish, shimmering with golden scales, and she was very surprised; where in the world had there ever been such fish? She fished out a few, but she knew that the fish died as soon as they left the water, and even more strangely, the golden little fish had become lumps of gold! She was happy and astonished, thinking that it must be divine help. She ran to tell her mother, and turned back to turn the gold into rice. After that, her family gradually became a prosperous family because of the goldfish in this stream. Unexpectedly, they later leaked this matter to the outside world, and people from far and near came to snatch the goldfish. The strong beat the weak, and the young killed the old. At this time, Heaven knew again, probably using some immortal magic, from then on, the fish in the water were goldfish, and on the shore they were still goldfish, but the gold color of these goldfish could not be sold like gold.

()

Miss L once sat on the table wearing shorts, her trousers rolled up, completely exposing one leg of white flesh. Her friend T warned her:

"Hey! What do you look like?"

L understood the meaning of these words, and she pulled a face and said:

"Why do you put your hand outside? Isn't it just a piece of meat like my leg!"

Everyone was silent. A kind of worldly pseudo-moral observation is really ridiculous. During the day, they really say "etiquette is strict," and at night? I don't believe they don't secretly grope with their wives.

Amateur Ramblings

To Have Peace in the World, Everyone Must Have Food to Eat 262

— Han Dehui

The Amateur Weekly, at the expense of its precious space, has specially opened a "Self-Employment Introduction" column for the unemployed. This enthusiasm is already worthy of our admiration; and the editor often gives up the position of "Editor's Surplus" to publish many free advertisements introducing occupations, which is even more touching!

In these free advertisements, we see many job seekers. Some who have served as editors and teachers are now willing to take the position of a chauffeur; some who are proficient in handling books and bookkeeping are now willing to serve as a tea room worker or errand boy; there are even university students who do not care about salary and sell themselves at any price. To these poor friends, in addition to expressing "sympathy for each other" and my own feeling of "fellow sufferers," I also feel that I myself am now in a small occupation and have not been squeezed into the ranks of the unemployed and gone to the hunger line, so I cannot help but shout "Lucky!", || although my current small occupation can only be called half-hungry and half-full.

"Unemployment" is indeed a very serious problem in our China, no, the whole world today. If this serious problem is not properly resolved and allowed to become more and more serious day by day, I don't know what a tragic result it will lead to in the future!

Although I am deeply indignant for the poor friends who are unemployed and have no food to eat, I am also deeply worried for the old masters, ladies, young masters, and young ladies who live in luxury and extravagance. If you really force them to be unable to survive and let them starve to death, they will never let you have a good time at that time; because they also have the right to survive in this world!

Even if one person is in distress, the whole table will be unhappy; can you not be moved when you see so many of the same kind, with the same round heads and square feet, suffering hardship and on the verge of death!

In my opinion, for the sake of self-interest and the benefit of others, you should not ignore this serious problem of "unemployment." Everyone should work hard day and night to find a proper solution as soon as possible!

To have peace in the world, everyone must have food to eat. Although we cannot reach the ideal of sharing blessings together for the time being, at the very least, we cannot allow there to be an unemployed person in the world, that is to say, we cannot allow there to be a hungry person in the world.

Problem Discussion

The Problem of Improving the Lives of Female Workers in Hell 263

— Zong Wen

It is strange that female workers account for more than half of the workers in so many factories in Shanghai. This is not necessarily a bad phenomenon. Who says that women's careers in society are not developed? The wages of male workers are already low enough, but the wages of female workers are about a dime less than those of male workers, so that they cannot even get enough to eat after working hard all day long. As for working hours, some are as long as fourteen hours. The first steam pipe rings at five o'clock every morning, and they get up to eat breakfast; the second steam pipe rings at half past five, and the factory gate opens, and they enter the factory; the third steam pipe rings at six o'clock, and the factory gate closes, and they start work: they take a one-hour break at twelve o'clock for lunch: they go back to work at one o'clock in the afternoon, and do not stop until five or six o'clock in the evening. In the yarn factory, the machines run day and night. In addition, there are night shifts. Although night shifts have extra wages, many female workers often do it to exhaustion and die from overwork in order to get more wages. This is really a terrible thing!

The rules of the factory are very strict. The foremen are all like wolves and tigers, domineering and doing whatever they want: they often beat and scold the workers unreasonably, deduct their wages, or even fire them; what is especially hateful is that they arbitrarily check the workers at the factory gate when they leave work, simply playing with them for pleasure.

When they come home from work every day, they also have to cook and prepare meals, raise sons and daughters, and wash the whole family's clothes. 365 days a year, they simply have no time to rest except for a few hours of sleep. So their suffering is even greater than that of male workers.

Women have a natural love for beauty, but the female workers are limited by economics and cannot get full development, and because of economic oppression, many female workers often fall and engage in prostitution as well.

Alas! The lives of female workers are really too pitiful! How should it be improved? I hope that all the readers of this journal will discuss it together.

Life in the Industrial and Commercial World

The Bleak Life of a Small Company Employee Amidst Wind and Rain 264

— Destroyed Respect

『Old B! Old B!』

A, lying in bed, seemed to hear the rain falling, and felt troubled in his stomach, calling out to B, who was sleeping on the bed opposite him.

Although B was awakened by A’s call, he was too lazy to speak, only shifting his body slightly in the bed.

『Old B! Listen! It sounds like it’s raining!』 A called out again.

『Really?』 B suddenly poked his head out and, after listening carefully, said, 『My goodness! It’s really raining hard!』

『Damn! Damn!』 A and B sighed in unison.

A and B were both small employees in the company, receiving meager salaries and living a life that was neither rich nor poor, a precarious existence for the petty bourgeoisie.

Page 20

They sighed when they heard the rain. There was a reason for this.

A often divided their monthly life into four eras, much like historians divide past historical facts into different periods. This was based on his own economic principles.

A said: The first week after receiving his salary is called the “Silver Dollar Era,” because during this era, payments for meals, rent, debt, and sometimes even buying a pair of shoes are all made with silver dollars. That's why it's called the "Silver Dollar Era." In the second week, although there aren't many silver dollars left, they're converted into dimes, and there are still a few. Buying two chocolate bars or taking a rickshaw twice allows one to feel a little comfortable. The spending is mostly in dimes. By the third week, only copper coins are used. At most, one might spend a hundred copper coins to buy some roasted chestnuts. During this "Copper Coin Era," one can still scrape by. But by the fourth week, the wallet is empty. Even the tram fare is difficult to come by, so one has to "eat tomorrow's rations today," borrowing from here and there. This "Eating Tomorrow's Rations" era is quite miserable.

『Damn! In this "Eating Tomorrow's Rations" era when we don’t even have tram fare, Heaven still has to rain!』 A shouted bitterly in bed.

·····························

Time passed silently, still passing, passing, passing. The small hand of the clock pointed straight at eight o’clock. The sound of wind and rain was particularly loud, penetrating through the window lattice. A and B had no choice but to get up.

Fifteen minutes later, A and B, wearing galoshes and desperately holding umbrellas, walked with great difficulty through a fierce wind and rain. Although the lower part of their robes was already wet, they still struggled to run towards the Bund.

Life as a Messenger

A Special Class Among Servants 265

— Shi Bin

Being a messenger is a special class among servants. Their duties involve both internal and external affairs. They have to deliver letters and organize all the miscellaneous tasks in the company. This would seem to indicate that their lives are very busy. In fact, most messengers have an easier life than those friends who bury themselves in paperwork all day long. When there are letters to deliver, they go out for a run, and when they come back, they do some cleaning. During their free time, they gather together and engage in lively discussions. Their lives are much more relaxed than ours, sitting at a desk all day, becoming as silent as cicadas when we see Western bosses. Even in terms of salary, some clerks earn less than they do.

There is no fixed standard for messengers' salaries. Generally, it is determined by the number of years of service. Some messengers who have worked for more than ten years earn around one hundred yuan. This amount is certainly not large compared to the income of the average merchant, but we must understand that their income does not rely entirely on a fixed salary. What they value most is the extra income. Sometimes the extra income can even exceed the fixed salary. For example, during lunar festivals, the festival bonuses given by the clerks in large offices or companies can sometimes amount to seventy or eighty yuan per messenger, making them much happier than those friends who are desperate at every festival. Even in ordinary times, many import and export merchants distribute extra income at the end of each month, and messengers are also included in the distribution.

In addition to the above two sources of income, messengers who are good at making money sometimes also engage in other businesses, such as selling sweets or snacks, and in the summer, they sell soda or "Beauty" brand ice cream, catering to the needs of the clerks. This is also a great way to make money.

The life of a messenger is indeed carefree, but sometimes it is also risky. For example, some old messengers with established credit often have to carry thousands of silver dollars to the bank for deposit or withdrawal. A moment of carelessness can easily lead to problems. Fortunately, their simple clothing does not attract the attention of criminals, otherwise, they would suffer.

Messengers are also known as "coolies," and sometimes they are called "boys." But both of these terms are not very accurate. Think about it, although they are laborers, they are not as hardworking as porters. As for "boy," it is the general term used by Westerners for all servants. But if you think about it carefully, messengers are at least thirty years old, which is not qualified to be called "boy," while the "boy" referred to by Westerners refers to general younger trainees or waiters in bars.

Amateur Coffee House Intellectuals Show Signs of Hunger 266

— Li Tong

"Do not laugh at the farmer's cloudy rice wine,

A bountiful year leaves guests satisfied with chicken and pork."

丨Lu Fangweng

Indeed, everyone can easily achieve sufficient food and clothing, drink enough old wine, say a few sarcastic remarks, and write a few boring poems. Accommodate guests? Rice wine? Chicken and pork? To be honest, with the rural economy completely ruined today, the reality tells us that these are long impossible. Like my uncle in the countryside used to brew yellow wine every year, but in recent years, even the jar for yellow wine is nowhere to be found. Strange? I asked him why he didn't make yellow wine these years, he didn't say anything, just sighed:

"Brewing wine? It's not easy! Where does the rice come from? The harvest from the fields is not enough for our own family to eat. In good years, an average of four dan of grain is harvested per mu, but in bad years, even two or one dan cannot be harvested. Even with the current cheap rice price, each hu only sells for four or five yuan, and we still have to deduct the landlord's rent, soybean cake money, and various land taxes and household taxes... One mu can only be sold for more than ten yuan. Think about it, after deducting so much money, is there any room for profit? I am sixty years old this year and have never seen such a pressing situation as in recent years. When I was young, a pig's head at the butcher's only sold for more than two hundred wen, and the rent was only seven hundred wen per mu. If one was unfortunately ill, hiring a doctor only cost one or two hundred wen. The standard of living was so low, but by the end of the year, many families still couldn't make ends meet! Borrowing money, repaying debts, pawning clothes... In recent years, alas! Even more so..."

The elderly uncle certainly wouldn't tell me any lies. Look, how declining is the current rural situation! Accommodate guests? I ask, what can they use to accommodate them?

The aggression and oppression of the great powers, the endless civil wars of the warlords, the capitalists ruthlessly exploiting the blood and sweat of a group of pitiful workers, the corrupt officials greedily scraping the fat off countless impoverished farmers, everything, everything is about to end the lives of the working masses!

Mencius said: "If the kitchen is full of fat meat, and the stable is full of fat horses, but the people have a hungry look, and the fields are full of starving corpses, this is leading beasts to devour men!" This is a good portrayal of the current society.

Literary Works

On the Road to Baiquan 267

— Wang Chanmo

At this time, it was about four o'clock in the afternoon. Lead-colored dark clouds filled the sky. Snowflakes were rolled into balls by the roaring northwest wind and fell down. The ground was almost a foot thick. The road to Baiquan was all white. Not to mention seeing any people, there wasn't even a single bird or beast. However, in a large forest, not far from the main road in the middle, there seemed to be more than three hundred people dressed in white scattered on both sides, each with a very anxious look on their faces, as if they had made an appointment with friends, and the friends hadn't arrived after the appointed time, and they were feeling anxious.

"It's getting late, why haven't they come yet? Could it be that the reporter got the date wrong?"

"That's right? We received orders yesterday afternoon to come here and ambush. It was said that today, at the latest by lunchtime, those shorties would be here. Why haven't they come yet?"

"Could it be that the shorties already know?"

"Impossible, right? Look, there's so much snow, there's not a single trace on the road, and the planes haven't come to scout either, how would they know we're waiting for them here?"

"This is really strange. The road to Baiquan has to go through here. Otherwise, the reporter must have made a mistake."

"Stop arguing, listen, what's that sound?"

"It doesn't sound like a plane, it must be a truck carrying pigs!"

"That's right, these shorties must have come after eating their fill, planning to go to Baiquan tonight and fight us..."

The sound of the truck moving on the snow, cha...cha...cha..., and the vibration of the motor mixed with the northwest wind, were carried over from afar. These brothers perked up their ears like hunting dogs and listened. Sure enough, the sound was getting closer and closer. The hot blood in everyone's veins was immediately ignited by the excitement of killing the enemy, and their eyes sparkled with brave and joyful light. They exchanged knowing smiles. On the order, the brothers on both sides prepared their weapons, waiting for the enemy to come and die.

Five trucks and two armored vehicles entered the forest, tail to tail like a long snake. On the five trucks, there were about thirty Japanese soldiers on average per vehicle, all with their necks shrunk, chattering and laughing. The first armored vehicle led the way into the forest. After only a short distance, the last armored vehicle was also within the firing line of the brothers ambushing on both sides. The brothers all had their fingers on the triggers, thinking that whoever's bullet flew out first would determine the fate of those things. However, they were still waiting, waiting, waiting for the commander's order - waiting for the first mortar shell to fire, which would be their chance.

The vehicles had already reached the area completely surrounded by the brothers. The first armored vehicle fell into the hole that they had dug in advance. At that moment, a deafening sound broke the silence on the road to Baiquan. A shell flew onto the armored vehicle and destroyed the engine. Before the enemy could retaliate, another shell flew from the right and blew away all the objects in front of the vehicle.

Caught in this unexpected attack, the enemy panicked and scrambled to grab their guns and set up their machine guns. As they jumped out of the vehicles and scattered around them to fight back, forty or fifty of the enemy had already had their bodies become the permanent resting place for lead bullets. The targets of our four mortars were all on those seven vehicles, so except for the machine guns on the two armored vehicles still firing in all directions, the five trucks were completely destroyed.

After this mutual bombardment for a long time, night had fallen, and specks of fire sparkled in the darkness. The smell of sulfur choked everyone. The machine guns on the two armored vehicles could not withstand the concentrated artillery fire and were soon destroyed. Following this, the enemy's firepower was not as strong as before. On the commander's order to charge, the brothers flanked from both sides. Rain-like lead bullets were fired densely towards the enemy, and the magnificent shouts of killing shook the snowy night like thunder...

The enemy didn't know how many of our brothers there were, only feeling that bullets were flying from all directions. In the beginning, before the machine guns on the two armored vehicles were destroyed, although they were afraid, they still hoped that the armored vehicles could charge forward and open a bloody path. But after the machine guns on the armored vehicles stopped firing, they were completely disappointed and knew that today the chance of death was greater than the hope of survival. When our brothers charged, the enemy, half of whom were already dead, struggled under a barrage of intense fire for a while. Suddenly, the bullets from the opposite side stopped flying over. They only heard a chaotic and rapid sound of footsteps on the snow. They saw the flashing broadswords reflecting the snow and emitting a cold light. So the enemy's machine guns and rifles all stepped up their firing, hoping to repel the brothers who were charging over. Our brothers fell in one row, and immediately another row filled in, wielding broadswords and holding grenades. Row after row, they stepped over the corpses of their own brothers and charged forward. Some of the enemy's machine guns were destroyed by grenades, and some were seized by the brothers, who turned the muzzles and swept them at the enemy. The flashing light of the swords splashed the blood of the Yamato spirit and sprinkled it on the white snow, a strange and bright color...

The sound of gunfire gradually thinned out... and finally stopped completely. While rescuing the wounded brothers, a smug smile appeared on the face of each brother.

Snowflakes were still rolled into balls by the roaring northwest wind and fell down. On the road to Baiquan, a team of more than two hundred people was walking, trampling on the snow, cha...cha...cha.......

Self-Employment Advertisement

Buy One Get Two Free 268

— Lin

The owner of a store, because business was slow, had to engage in a large-scale sale, and advertised with a big sign saying "Buy One Get One Free," hoping that the goods in his store would be sold immediately.

I have always worked in administrative agencies, serving in "As Directed" and "Similar Reasons" positions. I have served as a section chief and director for ten years. I believe that my strengths lie in being responsible and having quick writing skills. I also have experience in handling official documents. Now, because business is slow, I have decided to imitate the store's method and borrow space in this column to post an advertisement (fortunately, there is no advertising fee), implementing "Buy One Get Two Free," which is even cheaper than the store.

As for the "Buy One Get Two Free" method, my previous job paid at least one hundred yuan per month. Now, as long as I receive more than thirty yuan, I can take on six or seven hours of work a day. If the time is reduced, I am willing to reduce the compensation accordingly. All can be discussed in person. My agency is located in the editorial department of this publication. Please buy quickly! Buyers can be from any organization or store, but those in other cities must add a reasonable compensation. All kinds of certificates are complete and can be verified during contact.

A Joke 269

— Yang

From foreign news, we know that in European and American countries, regardless of politics and society, they are exhausting their wisdom to seek methods of relief for unemployed workers. The failure to satisfactorily resolve this issue can cause high-ranking officials to worry and the entire government to collapse. In our China today, this can only be told as a joke, and it is even more unnecessary to talk about it for other unemployed people.

I should first thank the editor of this publication, who can actually focus on the suffering of us unemployed people and is willing to set aside some valuable space to provide us with self-employment opportunities. Although I haven't gotten a good job yet, I first want to bless our editor!

Since the Japanese cannons of January 28th bombed away my only property and also bombed away my job, or rather, it can be said that I lost it myself. At that time, I was working in the Japanese-owned Shen Heng Foreign Firm on Jiangxi Road in this city, managing all the accounts. After the cannon fire of January 28th sounded, I felt that it was too heartless to be friends with the enemy again and to help the enemy as a pioneer in economic aggression. I was extremely ashamed. In order to prolong a few lives, I had lived under the enemy's fence for many years. At this time, although my family was ruined and my economy was in extreme panic, in order to fight for a little dignity for the country and fight for a little personality for the nation, I resolutely resigned from the Shen Heng Foreign Firm and was unwilling to cooperate with them anymore. Although many friends advised me to find another job before resigning, I wouldn't listen. Moreover, at that time, there were many enthusiastic patriotic organizations, such as the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, willing to be the backing for us generally unemployed people due to the anti-Japanese war. They asked me to register in order to introduce me to a job, and I did so. Who knew that after the sound of the cannons of January 28th subsided, the so-called Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association gradually faded away imperceptibly. I anxiously hoped at home every day that the association could truly fulfill its promise and give me a gospel of relief. But the true five-minute enthusiasm has passed, who is still shouldering the banner of Anti-Japanese National Salvation to shout again? My hope is forever just hope. I am still sitting at home, becoming a vague unemployed person, alas! It's been more than a year!

I am a high school graduate and have a considerable foundation in Japanese and English. Before entering Shen Heng, I also worked in a certain foreign firm managing accounts, so I am relatively good at handling new and old bookkeeping. If there are ordinary affairs, I am also willing to serve sincerely. I am looking forward to good news from any quarter in this publication.

Street Corners, Alleys, and The Great Evening News 271

Last night, I was walking home from the office and reached the intersection of Lyuban Road when I suddenly heard a loud call:

"The Great Evening News! Three copper coins a copy."

Then a thing that seemed black but not black, seemed white but not white waved in front of me. I stared at it: it turned out to be a child of about ten years old, holding a stack of newspapers in his left hand, and waving another one in his right hand in front of me. Just then, a smaller child ran up from the right, waving in the same way, shouting in the same way:

"The Great Evening News! Three copper coins a copy."

Great, this spirit of competition! I deliberately asked the two children: "I only need to buy one copy, but which one should I buy it from?" The older child said without competition: "We are brothers, you should buy it from him." This right, the older child was actually willing to give it to his brother, unwilling to create a "fratricidal" drama, how does that compare to the uncles and nephews of the two Liu's in Sichuan?

Those familiar with Ningbo people in Shanghai and those who have social skills, regardless of gender, can apply. Remuneration is mainly on a commission basis, and no position is given. For example, if you get one monthly subscriber, you will be paid one dime, 1.2 yuan per year. If you have 100 monthly subscribers, you can get 10 yuan. A guarantor or cash is required for the guarantee. I hope Mr. can do his best to introduce it. I respectfully greet you. Yang Dehui respectfully.

Shop Assistants' Correspondence: The Future of This Publication 272

To Mr. Pu, editor of the Amateur Weekly:

I am an out-of-town reader of your publication in the last two issues. Because I saw that the main articles of your publication are signed with the word "Pu," I shout out the above title, is it not wrong?

Because I admire your publication to one hundred and twenty points, and at the same time, I am limited by the area and cannot subscribe directly, so I wrote a letter to Mr. Shi Liangcai, the general manager of your newspaper, asking him to expand your publication to other cities, not to be confined to one corner, so that we out-of-town Shen Bao readers can enjoy the benefits of reading (the original letter is presented). We know that this is a matter of distribution and not within the power of Mr., so I will not talk too much.

But for the editorial aspect, I also have a request:

I ask you to publish as many articles as possible from us shop assistants, so that the suffering we endure has an opportunity to voice and vent. Usually, shop assistants have some difficult secrets for managers and bosses, but they are afraid of losing their jobs, so they dare not speak out publicly, only resent behind their backs. Therefore, I have no choice but to hope that your publication can be our spokesperson, a guarantor of the interests of us shop assistants. Although I know that under the current social system, the threshold of the school is very high. Without the white ocean dollars to cushion our feet, we cannot cross in. Therefore, the articles we write will certainly be a little unintelligible, and if they are published, it will inevitably collapse the stage of your publication. But with Mr.'s big axe, shaving and polishing for us, as long as it retains its essence, it is not impossible to publish it.

No matter what industry, large or small, it cannot be done well by the manager alone. They must rely on the shop assistants to be of one mind and cooperate fully in order to have the hope of prosperity and development. If the managers and bosses do not understand the suffering of the shop assistants, they are not concerned at all, and although the shop assistants do not say it, they harbor resentment in their hearts, then the future of this store is very dangerous. To avoid this danger, it is not effective to apply oppression. The best way is: let the shop assistants say what difficulties they have: let them contribute what suggestions they have: and the managers and bosses can also take this opportunity to study and improve the way to improve treatment. Isn't this much better than only knowing how to make money with your eyes closed, regardless of other people's lives and deaths, and ending up in bankruptcy?

I hope that Mr. can accept my request, and I hope that your publication will emit infinite light, guiding us distressed shop assistants out of the darkness:

Han Dehui Qiyi, Er, San, 273

Editor's Note: This publication has always focused on the interests of shop assistants, apprentices, and workers; therefore, in addition to the "Amateur Chats" and "Special Articles" columns, in order to solve their knowledge hunger, we have had to specially invite experts to write. Other columns such as "Problem Discussion," "Life in the Industrial and Commercial Circles," and "Shop Assistants' Correspondence" have always adopted articles from shop assistants. It is inevitable that some of the articles are of poor quality; however, as long as they have practical value, we always revise and publish them, and never dare to send them to the wastepaper basket. We firmly believe that only the shop assistants' own descriptions can be relevant; and only these relevant descriptions can touch the heartstrings of the shop owners. Therefore, we recently wrote "A Sketch of Life in the Wastepaper Basket" and "Congratulations on Getting Rich, Manuscripts Rolling In" in the editorial, just to hope that shop assistants will contribute more articles. Finally, we add a report that Mr. Shi, the president of our newspaper, has decided to accept Mr. Han's request and is preparing to expand this publication to other cities in the near future. At the same time, we should also cheer up and strive to enrich the quality of this publication.

Film Special Edition

Republic of China 22nd Year, February 12th, Sunday (No Extra Charge)

Charles Farrell and Janet Gaynor's Farewell 274

— Xi Rong

Charles Farrell and Janet Gaynor, the greatest screen lovers in Hollywood, hailed as the Emperor and Empress of film by the global film community, have now divorced on screen. Some may speculate that their on-screen partnership has fractured and their personal friendship has ended. However, such speculation is far from the truth. On the morning that Charles Farrell decided to leave Fox Studios and terminate his contract with studio manager Winfield Sheehan, many staff, actors, and workers gathered in front of Sheehan's office, having heard the bad news. They all thought Charles would change his mind, believing that his status and salary were enough to make him stay. But he resolutely and proudly canceled the contract.

Charles completed all the contract cancellation procedures. Of course, there were many handshakes and words of farewell and comfort. Charles then went to Janet Gaynor's studio to say goodbye to her. At that time, she was filming with a new male lead. Seeing Charles walk in, she immediately stopped working, ran to him, took his hand, and said, "Charles, are you leaving? You're leaving alone. From now on, I'll have to go on alone too." While speaking, Janet seemed to have a thousand words stuck in her throat, unable to express them all, and her eyes were filled with tears. It was a truly sorrowful parting! Afterwards, Charles told people that he had also choked up for a long time and couldn't speak. Judging by this emotional farewell, there was no rift between the two.

Why Charles wants to temporarily leave the screen can be said that he is no longer willing to continue working with Janet. However, he is not dissatisfied with Janet personally or anyone in the company, but rather with the roles he has been getting in the scripts. Because film scripts rarely have roles where both male and female leads are equally prominent, it's impossible to continue collaborating year after year. Therefore, since "Seventh Heaven," in all the films he has co-starred with Janet Gaynor, while Janet's reputation remains unwavering, Charles himself has gradually been relegated to a supporting role. This is something he cannot endure permanently.

Charles has no jealousy towards Janet's fame. He once said, "I would never want Janet to sacrifice her reputation to accommodate me. Her reputation has been built up painstakingly over the years. No one knows Janet better than I do in this regard." Therefore, he had to leave voluntarily.

As for the personal relationship between Charles and Janet, everyone probably knows that they both have families. Janet loves her husband deeply, just as Charles loves his wife deeply. They are among the most morally upright people in Hollywood. Their seven years as screen lovers have not affected their marital love within their families. Charles once said, "Between the two of us, there is the affection of siblings, brotherly and sisterly love, and we are friends who have gone through many hardships together. Our struggles, worries, disappointments, and hopes are shared. We can understand each other. We are considerate and helpful to each other's goals and desires. There is a deep and perfect relationship between us. In fact, there are no better friends on screen than the two of us. The reason lies in our 'honesty and selflessness.'"

From this, I can predict that they will still be able to collaborate in the future, but first they need a good script that allows Charles to regain his true character as Chico, and Janet to continue playing his Dianne.

Film Review

Review of "Such a Hero" by Ling He 丨 Premieres in Beijing 丨 275

Although I don't usually enjoy comedies, because China has produced an "Oriental Laurel and Hardy," and I am so concerned about the development of Chinese cinema, I naturally had to see this "great innovation in the Chinese film industry" that was being promoted in the newspapers.

However, this "great contribution" didn't impress me as much as they claimed. But out of a sincere hope for Chinese cinema, I have to be frank.

I have seen George Bernard Shaw's plays and Charlie Chaplin's cane and worn shoes. Although their works are humorous and comedic, even I, who am a complete amateur when it comes to comedy, feel that they have depth and are worth contemplating, even bringing tears to my eyes amidst laughter. I can't help but admire them; I have to admit that they are illuminators of life. However, this particular comedy, although its theme is to ridicule "heroes" and expose their true nature, unfortunately does not evoke any kind of stimulus in us.

The performance abilities of Liu Jiqun and Han Langen seem to be insufficient. Director Zhuang Guojun's assistance is also minimal, and in many places, we can see that the director's skills are not refined. The other supporting actors are all stiff, so people who are used to watching foreign slapstick films cannot help but feel bored. However, comparatively speaking, Liu Jiqun is better than Han Langen, because Mr. Han overacts.

In other aspects, the lighting is too dim, and the cinematography is not skillful. However, the subtitles are very well done.

However, the last few scenes are very good. The way the same actor cross-dresses as a woman and a child is indeed very interesting. Of course, this is due to the director's cleverness, but also to the efforts of the screenwriter.

I heard from a friend that this is much better than Liu Chunshan's "Chicken and Duck Couple," but I haven't seen "Chicken and Duck Couple." Moreover, since this is an "innovation" and has achieved this much, it is still quite satisfying, so I have great hope for their future.

Finally, because I followed many viewers in laughing for a while and still have the taste of laughter in my heart, I couldn't help but be a bit unrestrained in my sentence construction when writing this review. However, I have sincere intentions, which insightful readers should be able to understand.

Hollywood Rumors 276

— Jing Wu

Regarding Charles Farrell and Janet Gaynor

Hollywood rumors are truly bizarre. If you are a famous star, then there will be even more rumors about you. Charles Farrell is one of them.

After Charles Farrell finished filming "Street Angel," Hollywood rumors started, saying that he was in love with the female lead of "Street Angel," Joan Crawford, and that they often frequented cafes together, and the rumors were very convincing. But Charles just smiled and ignored them, and soon the rumors disappeared.

One rumor disappeared, and another one came. Hollywood rumored again. After Charles Farrell and Janet Gaynor finished filming "The First Year of Marriage" and "The Tide of Love," these rumors spread almost all over Hollywood. It was said that Janet and Charles's love was rekindling. Janet was going to divorce her husband, and Charles was also preparing to dissolve his marriage contract with his wife. As a result, many reporters went to Janet's place to interview her, which made Janet cry. She said, "Heavens! Why do so many people like to spread rumors like this? You know, my husband loves me very much." On Charles Farrell's side, he felt that this rumor was malicious. Later, many film publications dispelled the rumors for the two of them, and the rumor gradually disappeared.

Film and Literary Taste Huang Zhenxia (5) 277

— Yu

This is a dull, drizzly film. It depicts the dark side of the bright and beautiful islands of the South Seas, with the struggle between religion and desire. A pastor, a border guard, and a wandering woman of unknown origin form this pool of rainwater – a symbol of depression and lust.

Rain, always rain, the dull tropical rain of the South Seas, beating on banana leaves, drop by drop, like sorrowful tears, like greedy saliva, crawling into people's hearts like snakes. This is the suggestion the whole film gives us, but the performance is very dull and not deeply moving. Joan Crawford also tries hard but doesn't get good results, and every move is like an American hillbilly. Because she focuses too much on expressing local class colors, she loses universality, so Easterners don't find it very interesting. The depiction of religion is also a localized American style, so people don't feel the grandeur of Catholicism or the pure faith of Christianity. The director is also not a top talent, and the monotony and repetition are tiresome. A very good subject is ruined. From beginning to end, it's like reading a laborious realistic novel.

In addition, from an objective perspective, of course, half of the reason is that we don't understand American accents very well. Otherwise, we could just treat it as a stage play to "listen" to, and maybe we would be more satisfied? However, since the result is like this, then our sympathy for this film is only separated by the rain.

Mingyue Song and Dance Troupe's "Little Soldier, Little General." From right to left are Hu Jia, Yu Siyong, Chen Qing, Han Guomei, Bai Lizhu, Zhang Jing, and Yang Zhilu. Shanghai Jiang Photography Modern Gift

New Developments in "Screen Views" 278

"Screen Views," organized by Westerners McDonald and others, is dedicated to promoting the film industry and introducing screen news. It is published monthly, and five issues have been published so far. The sixth issue (February) is also published today. Its novel content and exquisite printing are well-received by all sectors. Starting from March, a Chinese version will be published for each issue. Its content is the same as the Western version, and it is planned to publish two issues per month in the shortest possible time.

Shenzhou Film Company Revived 279

— Hong

丨"King of Mines" to Start Filming

The Shenzhou Film Company has been dormant for a long time, but we can see the hard work of the personnel who came out of Shenzhou in the existing film companies. According to reliable information, Zhou Ke and others, former members of Shenzhou, have decided to revive Shenzhou and have selected a play with a mine as its background, named "King of Mines." The filming location has been selected in a mine in Anhui. The director is Zhou Ke, and the main actors have been hired as Gao Zhanfei, Wang Renmei, and Li Li. They will start working soon.

Film Repair Hospital 280

— Jiang Qing

In Broadway and many other large cities in the United States, the companies that manage the rental of films have specially hired many people to do film repair work. When repairing, one end of the film is rolled onto the reel of the repair machine, and the holes on both sides of the film are carefully checked for cracks and damage. If the film is broken or missing, it is also repaired. Usually, a set of films needs to be repaired after being shown more than four times. The cost of repair is very high. This business has been very developed recently. It can be said that these are two kinds of light jobs, and most of the workers are women.

Film Novel "Bill of Divorcement" (14) 281

— Yi

His painful cry forced her to go one step further. "Gray, my darling! I can't abandon him; he's so pathetic. He begged me not to go. If you heard him speak, if you saw his misery, you wouldn't bear to force me to go with you and leave this lonely man here. He'll go crazy again, you know? He says he loves me, always loves me. He makes me believe that if I leave, he won't live. Ah, Gray! He keeps tempting me like this, making me believe that if I'm not with him, he'll do something rash, and I'm too ____, and I end up believing he'll do it. Please, Gray, I simply can't bear to do this to you! I know my will is too weak, but please forgive me."

Margaret's frantic plea disturbed Gray's mind. He lowered his head, pondered for a while, and said firmly, "Margaret, I know your emotions right now, but if you truly love me, then come with me. You know how much I love you – I've waited for you for five whole years, and now is the time when our happiness can soon be realized. I will never give you up! Moreover, you've sacrificed your whole life for him, is he worth your sacrifice? Come on – I don't believe you've made the final decision to stay here with him. How can you suffer here for a lifetime? How can you love him like a wife should love her husband?"

Numbed and confused, Margaret said, "Ah, Gray, please don't say any more! How can you say such things? You know that I don't love anyone but you, but I can't, I can't bear to leave him!"

"And I will never leave you!" Gray said passionately.

⊙ ⊙ ⊙ ⊙

No one knew that Hillary had heard most of their conversation. When he arrived, he had stopped Dr. Han Lie at the door, wanting to take a walk on the grass first before going into the house. He saw two figures inside through the French windows and was about to go in and see when he heard Margaret's mournful cries and Gray's reply. So, he held back his steps and carefully considered what he had heard. But is it true? She has never sincerely loved him? She pities him, but doesn't love him! (To be continued)
